Foreign Important Telegrams

The War Debt Issue Will Take a Sudden Turn

The French Government Follows the British in Sending a Note to the US Government

President Hoover Reads the Dispatch and Sets Off to Return to Beijing

Foreign Minister Simon Meets with the French, Italian, and Belgian Ambassadors

National News Agency, November 11, Bar Harbor dispatch: President Hoover departed from here at 8:57 PM tonight to return to Beijing.

▲ Reuters, November 11, Washington dispatch: Secretary of State Stimson stated today that the British note regarding the war debt issue has been submitted to President Hoover and will likely not be released within two days. The French note to the US government regarding the war debt issue was received this evening and is largely similar to the British note.

▲ National News Agency, November 11, Washington dispatch: It is now confirmed tonight that the war debt issue will transcend the political realm and be based purely on the global economic situation for resolution. With the US government having received the British and French notes, there is no doubt that the war debt repayment methods will be revised.

Important French Financial Figures Gather in London

Reuters, November 11, London dispatch: Foreign Minister Sir John Simon has met with the French, Belgian, Italian, and other ambassadors to report on the contents of the British note to the US government regarding the war debt issue. It is rumored that the contents of the British note will be kept strictly confidential for the time being, pending Stimson's response before deciding whether to publish it. News from Paris states that the French government, following the British precedent, has also sent a note to the US government regarding the war debt issue, making certain claims. It is noted that the French debt to the US due this time is to be paid on February 15th of next year. Former French cabinet member and current chairman of the Finance Committee, Malvy, will come to London soon. His purpose may be to discuss extending the deadline for suspension of war debt payments before a formal war debt conference is held. In addition, former French Finance Minister Flandin will also come to England to meet with the British Trade Minister Runciman. The arrival of these figures in England is sufficient to show the importance attached to the war debt issue by all parties. So far, the French government has not expressed its attitude on the war debt issue, but Reuters' Paris reporter has learned that the financial attaché of the French Embassy in the United States has been ordered by the French government to request the US government to extend the deadline for suspension of war debt payments. ▲ Havas News Agency, November 11, Paris dispatch: Finance Minister Germain Martin, accompanied by senior officials from the Ministry of Finance, visited Prime Minister Herriot today to discuss the debt to the United States due on December 15th. After the discussion, the Finance Minister told people that the government had consulted with the United States on this matter, but due to diplomatic etiquette, it was not convenient to disclose the details.

▲ National News Agency, November 11, Washington dispatch: US President Hoover has prepared to return to Beijing. He received the British dispatch on reorganizing war debts at the Bar Harbor home. It is now reported that Secretary of State Stimson stated that after receiving the dispatch, he immediately forwarded it to the President. As for its content, Stimson refused to disclose or comment, but said that it would soon be announced simultaneously by the British and American governments. France and Italy have not yet sent dispatches to the United States, but it is expected that they will follow Britain soon, as Britain, adhering to its traditional policy and adding the results of the Lausanne Conference, occupies the leading position among debtor nations regarding the war debt issue.

During his speech accepting the Republican nomination for presidential candidate, President Hoover suggested that Britain grant the United States special trade rights to offset a portion of the war debt. However, the British government has not yet made a clear statement on this matter. Whether this suggestion was mentioned in the dispatch is currently being speculated by people in Washington, and they are eagerly awaiting the publication of the dispatch.

This debt is due on December 15th. Germany has already used the extension agreement to declare to the US government that it will postpone payment to Britain, while the British government has proposed reorganizing it in this dispatch. The British government owes the United States a total of 4.6 million US dollars in war debt, which is to be repaid in sixty-two years according to the war debt agreement, until it is cleared in 1984. So far, over 12.8614 million US dollars have been repaid. Now, many in the American financial and industrial circles also believe that the world's economy is difficult to fully recover when the British government and other foreign governments bear this debt. A few weeks ago, President Hoover also stated during his campaign speech that European countries are indeed unable to pay according to the current method. Therefore, it is believed here that the war debt issue will inevitably be subject to a new agreement and a new solution. However, the US President wants to consider each debtor country separately and opposes negotiating a general solution for all debtor countries together. European countries also know the President's intention, so Britain took the lead in submitting the proposal independently.

▲ National News Agency, November 11, Washington dispatch: It was learned tonight that France has also sent a dispatch to the US government proposing to reorganize the war debt issue. It is rumored that both the British and French dispatches will be sent to President-elect Roosevelt for consultation before the US government decides on its position. The contents of the French dispatch have not been published.

▲ Reuters, November 11, London dispatch: Sir Robert Kindersley arrived in Southampton, England from New York today. He briefly stated to reporters that he believed the United States would adopt a sympathetic and reasonable attitude towards the debt issue.

▲ Reuters, November 12, Washington dispatch: The fact that the British government has proposed the war debt issue shortly after the US presidential election has aroused considerable and cautious criticism here. Politicians say that the United States can gain something in return for revising European debts. President Hoover will take a short break after the election campaign and return to Washington within two days. The British document will be published simultaneously in Britain and the United States. Democratic Senator Robinson stated today that if the President declares that the current debt payment method is the final solution and cannot be changed, then the global economic situation can tend to stabilize and not cause so much turmoil.

▲ National News Agency, November 12, Washington dispatch: Senator Reed, as the President's personal representative, traveled to Europe. He has already declared that Congress may not approve of further extending the war debt issue. Even if the debtor countries default next Tuesday, he believes that Congress will immediately bring it up for discussion. Reed knows the attitude of Congress well and, as he represents the President after inspecting the European economic situation, his statements are often considered to have the President's approval. Now that Reed has stated that Congress does not approve of delaying, it is enough to punish the United States, which also wants to start talks with the debtor countries as soon as possible.

As for President Hoover, today he telegraphed that his special train would only stop briefly at Greendale to see his son, indicating that the President also believes that this matter must be paid attention to immediately, and he must explain his attitude when reporting on the state of the nation to Congress on December 5th.

It is expected that President-elect Roosevelt, along with his future Secretary of State and Secretary of the Treasury, will also participate in the discussion. The British and French dispatches to the US government decision may not be published temporarily, but will be disclosed when the President reports on the state of the nation to Congress, and the Democratic Party's attitude on this issue can also be learned at that time. It is heard that the Democratic Party's internal opinions are not yet fully consistent. For example, Smith advocates extending the repayment, even for one or two decades is fine, while other leaders support appropriate reductions. Before Roosevelt expresses his views to Hoover, he must first unify the party's views.

▲ National News Agency, November 11, Paris dispatch: The French government decided today to follow Britain's example and consult with the Washington government on the deferred payment of war debts. Part of the French debt to the United States, about 25 million US dollars, is due on December 15th. France plans to extend the payment period. The Paris newspaper "Le Matin" reported that the financial counselor of the French Embassy in Washington has contacted the US State Department to re-discuss the war debt issue.

Issue of Equality in Armaments

Foreign Minister Simon Will Go to Geneva

New British and French Proposals Can Be Submitted Soon

▲ National News Agency, November 11, Geneva dispatch: According to those familiar with the League of Nations, British Foreign Minister Simon will come to Geneva around Sunday or Monday to submit the British solution to the issue of equality in armaments to the main committee of the Disarmament Conference.

A new plan for French construction armaments and safety, etc., will also be passed by the French cabinet on Monday and will be sent simultaneously to the authorities in Geneva, Rome, London, Berlin, etc., around Thursday or Friday next week. As for the final negotiations on the issue of equality in armaments, it must wait until British Foreign Minister Simon, French Foreign Minister Herriot, and German Foreign Minister Neurath come here to participate in the League of Nations Administrative Council before they can be held.

Riots Occur on Armistice Day

South Irish Republican Army Clashes with Police

Communists and Royalists Clash in Paris

Havas News Agency, November 11, Paris dispatch: Today, the 14th anniversary of the Armistice was held here with extremely grand ceremonies. All institutions, shops, and most civilian homes hung national flags to express celebration. The morning was foggy. Government personnel gathered in front of the Arc de Triomphe, and the onlookers on both sides were crowded. At around 11 o'clock, President Lebrun arrived by car, first shaking hands with the speakers of both houses of parliament and cabinet members, and then taking off his hat and walking to the Tomb of the Unknown Soldier to pay his respects. The tomb was filled with wreaths. After a minute of silence, General Giraud conducted the military parade. Participants included students from the École Polytechnique, the Saint-Cyr Military Academy, various army, navy, and colonial troops, and motorcycle teams. During the ceremony, several reserve officers held war-damaged military flags and joined the parade. After the event, they were returned to the Les Invalides for display. People who paid their respects to the Tomb of the Unknown Soldier continued into the evening.

▲ National News Agency, November 11, Dublin dispatch: A major riot occurred here on Armistice Day. More than a thousand members of the Irish Republican Army marched through the streets, burning British flags, snatching poppies worn by passersby, singing "We will crown Valera as King of Ireland," and shouting "Dublin does not need to wear poppies!" (Note: This flower is a symbol of peace.) During the disturbance, many small shops were vandalized, and cars were overturned, with people dragged out and beaten. The authorities then ordered the mobilization of the security team, along with the police, to surround the disturbed area and carry out suppression. It is heard that after the melee, a total of twenty-six people were injured and sent to the hospital.

▲ National News Agency, November 12, Dublin dispatch: Police stated that one person died and several were arrested during yesterday's riots. The demonstrators resisted for four hours. Finally, the police were forced to fire blank shots, and the crowd dispersed. At that time, several women and children were squeezed to the ground and trampled.

▲ National News Agency, November 11, Dublin dispatch: Several thousand members of the South Irish Republican Army gathered in Dublin today to march through the streets, causing disruption. The police then mobilized all personnel to prevent the Republican Army's march and dispersed their ranks with batons. The Republican Army then smashed the glass windows of shops displaying poppies with bricks. Precautions were particularly strict at night. The central area of Dublin was surrounded. Many people were injured and sent to the hospital, and several were arrested. General Mulcahy, a supporter of the opposition party Cosgrave, protested in parliament against the government's threat to execute Cosgrave and others. Valera replied that the government would use all its power to maintain the right to freely discuss public issues and would not allow individuals or private groups to perform functions belonging to the state.

▲ Havas News Agency, November 11, Paris dispatch: Today is the 14th anniversary of the Armistice. This afternoon, peace activists, socialists, communists, and royalists all gathered their followers to hold demonstrations in front of the statue of the famous socialist leader Jaurès at the Panthéon. First, the peace activists placed a "palm of glory" in front of the statue. When the socialists did the same, a conflict broke out between the communists and royalists, and the order was disrupted. The police dispersed them. The royalists regrouped and seven people were arrested. The communists then flocked to the city hall, which was farther away, intending to regroup there, but they were prevented due to the precautions. Other than that, nothing else happened.

Turmoil in Geneva

The 24-Hour General Strike Has Begun

National News Agency, November 12, Bern dispatch: The situation in Geneva has suddenly deteriorated. The turmoil on Wednesday may extend elsewhere. Yesterday, the Zurich public meeting passed a resolution supporting the Socialists and Communists of Geneva, and the Zurich Communists even announced a general strike. However, whether the workers will comply is not yet certain. The 24-hour general strike in Geneva today has begun. Except for the railroad and tram workers, all other workers have joined. The state's Third Infantry Regiment and 103rd Reserve Regiment have been dispatched by the authorities to the villages this morning to sound horns and drums to summon mobilization. However, the mobilization notices posted in the city were quickly torn down by the workers. The Vaud region, a French-speaking area of the state, has also dispatched an infantry regiment to garrison the Geneva train station, while the Lausanne authorities have dispatched the 8th Cavalry Regiment to garrison the Mouji area, where the Lausanne-Geneva railway line connects. These troops are all under the command of Colonel York. All opinions everywhere say that the situation in Switzerland has never been as dangerous as it is today. If a serious conflict occurs between the workers and soldiers in Geneva, it is feared that bloody riots will also erupt in other industrial centers.

▲ Reuters, November 11, Geneva dispatch: The trade union committee notified the entire Geneva region that it would stage a 24-hour general strike tomorrow to protest the official handling of the Geneva disturbances this week. It has been investigated that twelve people died and about sixty were injured during the disturbances. The riots were caused by a conflict between the crowd and socialist leaders. The police were unable to stop it, so they mobilized troops to suppress it. However, the rioters attacked the army and seized their guns. Although the army retreated, they were still pursued by the rioters. The army then opened fire with machine guns on the crowd, causing several deaths and injuries.

▲ Reuters, November 12, Geneva dispatch: Since the Socialists wanted to petition the League of Nations for peace and disarmament, they were stopped by the police, which led to the major conflict on Wednesday. Today, the workers' groups have announced a general strike on Saturday for all private enterprises and Geneva tram workers, involving nearly 10,000 people. To prevent further disturbances, the authorities have ordered all troops and reserves to mobilize, and another cavalry regiment will be dispatched to Geneva tomorrow morning at 7:00 AM to strengthen the force. It is also heard that troops have been sent to patrol the streets of Lausanne, but no disturbances have occurred so far. The authorities anticipate that there will be some demonstrations when the general strike begins, so they are taking strict precautions and warning residents not to go out during the march.

▲ Reuters, November 12, Geneva dispatch: The main committee of the Disarmament Conference met today under the protection of Swiss army machine gunners to discuss ways to make disarmament a reality. This strange situation is due to the Geneva trade union's announcement of a general strike today. The Swiss authorities have mobilized four infantry battalions and a reserve battalion to prevent further riots. Tunnels carrying machine guns are hidden in the gardens of the League of Nations headquarters to prevent demonstrations against the League of Nations. So far, the response to the general strike has been sparse. The trams are still running as usual, and there is very little panic on the streets except for the presence of troops.

Netherlands Increases Tariffs

▲ Reuters, November 11, The Hague dispatch: It was learned today that the Dutch government will levy a 20% import tax on sugar to make up for the budget. Import taxes will also be levied on other goods, but limited to those that the Netherlands cannot produce.

The Disaster in Cuba is Extremely Severe

Twenty-Foot Waves Penetrate Inland

The Death Toll Exceeds Two Thousand Seven Hundred

National News Agency, November 11, Havana dispatch: After Cuba's southern coast suffered a catastrophic hurricane, the government announced today that the death toll has exceeded 1,500 and the number of injured is similar. Santa Clara Province reported 1,200 deaths, and all industries have stopped. Disaster reports from other places are still coming to Beijing, and it is feared that the total number of deaths and injuries will far exceed the aforementioned number. The government is organizing rescue teams to rush to the disaster area with medicine and food for emergency rescue.

▲ Reuters, November 11, New York dispatch: A dispatch from Camagüey, Cuba, states that Santa Cruz was the epicenter of the hurricane. Dozens of injured people from that area have arrived here by car. At least a thousand people have died in the storm. According to the latest news, two hundred and sixty bodies have been buried in Santa Cruz, and hundreds more remain in the forests and rubble. About four hundred people have been injured. No houses there are intact. Sea waves twenty feet high were whipped up by the wind and penetrated fifteen miles inland, causing many deaths and injuries. The disaster victims who arrived in Camagüey described the disaster as extremely tragic, saying that the hurricane began at dawn on Wednesday, the tide surged over the dike and flooded the city, with a water depth of twenty-one feet. About seventy ships were lost in the storm. The storm in Jamaica was also severe, but the disaster situation is unknown due to the lack of telephone communication. The weather is now fine, and traffic is expected to resume soon.

▲ Havas News Agency, November 12, Camagüey, Cuba, dispatch: The death toll from the storm is currently estimated to be about 2,700. The worst-hit areas are the provinces of Santa Cruz del Sur and Guáimaro in eastern Camagüey, as well as Long Island and Rum Cay in the Bahamas. The city of Santa Cruz has become a wasteland. After urgently recruiting burial workers, they found hundreds of corpses and cremated them all to prevent the spread of epidemics. According to a telegram sent by the British ship "Frosvik," Camagüey Island was completely destroyed, with about sixty residents killed and hundreds injured. The New York "Journal of Commerce" estimates that the loss from this storm will reach as much as 5 million US dollars.

The Bolivia-Paraguay War Continues

Reuters, November 11, Asunción dispatch: It is rumored here that Bolivian troops engaged Paraguayan troops in the Chaco forest yesterday. Three hundred and fifty Bolivian soldiers were killed.

The Japanese Emperor Falls Ill During Military Review

Reuters, November 12, Tokyo dispatch: According to the Imperial Household Ministry, the Japanese Emperor is currently reviewing troops in Osaka and has contracted a minor cold, which is not a cause for concern.

▲ Japan Allied News Agency, November 12, Tokyo dispatch: The Japanese Emperor was originally scheduled to oversee the army's large-scale exercise at the field headquarters today, but he decided to cancel the trip to the field due to a slight illness last night.

The United States Budget Deficit

Reaches Eight Hundred and Fifty Million

Tax Revenue Can Increase by Thirty Million After Repealing Prohibition

Reuters, November 12, Washington dispatch: It is estimated that the US budget deficit at the end of the current fiscal year will reach at least 850 million US dollars. Congress will have to implement a manufacturer's sales tax during the December session. Senator Reed stated today that the useless taxes under current law have failed to generate the necessary revenue.

▲ Reuters, November 11, Washington dispatch: Before the Democrats take over both houses of Congress, Congress will hold one more session, lasting three months. It is expected that there will be some disputes between the political parties. The House of Representatives, with a small Democratic majority, and the Senate, with a Republican majority, must consider the ordinary annual expenditure bill, tax cuts, and the prohibition issue. There will be heated debates on these matters. More than a hundred congressmen have been defeated in this election, and they will no longer be members after the new government takes office in March next year. Therefore, they will undoubtedly deliberately engage in strange tricks in the next meeting. According to the Tax Commission, the government can increase its revenue by 300 million US dollars annually after taxing the sale of beer and light wine.

The World News Agency said that in the US election, the Democrats won, and the prohibition is likely to be relaxed. According to opponents of the US prohibition, there are great economic losses. The New York statistician Mr. Teledt has created a table of prohibition losses, which is recorded as follows:

219,000 lawbreakers caused by prohibition, 200,000 bootleggers, £92,000,000 annual cost of enforcing prohibition, £200,000,000 annual loss of federal revenue, £4,000,000 annual loss of state revenue, £4,600,000 annual loss of city revenue, 170,000 people imprisoned for prohibition violations, 700,000 people unemployed due to prohibition, 23% increase in mental illness caused by illegally produced spirits.

Democratic Party Completely

Controls U.S. Congress

Kuomintang News Agency, Washington, 11th—According to the results of the Senate and House of Representatives elections announced today, which can be considered final, the Democratic Party has achieved a great victory. In the 73rd Congress, the Democratic Party will have 185 more seats than the opposition party in the House of Representatives. The new House breakdown is as follows: Democratic Party, 310 seats; Republican Party, 120 seats; Farmer-Labor Party, 5 seats. Among the 48 states, 28 states elected representatives entirely from the Democratic Party, which is expected to set a new record. In addition, 17 states, while not entirely Democratic, have at least one member from that party. Furthermore, the five members of the Farmer-Labor Party were all elected from Minnesota. Although there are still some close vote counts that need to be recounted, it is not expected to affect the established outcome. In the Senate, which has a total of 96 seats, the Democratic Party also has 22 more seats than the opposition party. The new Senate breakdown after March 4th will be as follows: Democratic Party, 59 seats; Republican Party, 36 seats; Farmer-Labor Party, 1 seat.

Matsuoka Arrives in Paris

Debuchi Returns to America to Resume Post

China United News Agency, Tokyo, 12th—Matsuoka Yosuke arrived in Paris, the French capital, at 11:45 this morning. He immediately invited Lieutenant General Tatekawa, Ambassador Matsudaira, Ambassador Sato, Sugimura (Deputy Foreign Minister), Tsuchibashi (Army Representative), and Umino (Navy Representative) to discuss countermeasures. It is reported that new strategies will be determined based on the instructions received by Matsuoka, taking into account the situations in various European and American countries.

▲ Dentsu News Agency, Hamburg, 11th—Representative Matsuoka, who is en route to Geneva, arrived in Hamburg at 11:00 PM today. He had lunch at the residence of Consul General Fujii in Hamburg with influential figures and important Japanese residents of the area. In the evening, he attended a dinner party hosted by Japanese residents and gave a speech on the situation in Manchuria. He departed Hamburg at 9:00 PM, heading directly to Paris via Berlin.

▲ Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 12th—Ambassador to the United States, Debuchi Katsuji, departed from Tokyo Station at 9:00 PM last night, traveling to America via Siberia and Europe to resume his post. The ambassador told reporters who visited him in the train that he had the opportunity to engage in sincere discussions with the government and various sectors of the public during his home leave and had gained much. Since the Manchurian Incident, relations between Japan and the United States have gradually deteriorated. However, Japan and the United States have close economic ties and have maintained the most intimate relationship for over half a century in other aspects. He believes that they will soon return to a friendly state. Although his return home was short, he personally inspected the solid development of Manchuria and gained much. After returning to his post, he plans to explain the freedom of Manchuria's independence and the relationship between Japan and Manchuria in detail to American officials and civilians, and strive for their understanding. He believes that the United States will be able to understand Japan's just position. When he arrives in Geneva, he will meet with various representatives, report on his discussions with Foreign Minister Uchida, and discuss everything frankly. He plans to go to Washington via England in mid-December.

▲ Japan United News Agency, Tsuruga, 12th—Ambassador to the United States, Debuchi Katsuji, arrived here this morning at around 8:00 AM with his wife, daughter, and secretary Sugahara. They transferred to the Amakusa Maru to Vladivostok and will return to their post via Europe.

▲ Havas News Agency, Paris, 13th—Matsuoka Yosuke, a member of the Japanese Lower House, former Vice President of the South Manchuria Railway, and current chief Japanese representative to the League of Nations, arrived in Paris at 11:20 AM today. The Japanese Ambassador to France, Nagaoka, the Ambassador to Belgium, Sato, the Minister to Switzerland, Yada, the Director of the Japanese Secretariat of the League of Nations, Sawada, and the Counselor of the Japanese Embassy in France all went to the Gare du Nord to greet him. Mr. Matsuoka, along with General Sato and Mr. Yosizawa, the former secretary of the Japanese Embassy in Berlin, stayed briefly in Berlin to meet with Mr. Ding Shiyuan, the representative of "Manchukuo" in Berlin, and to inquire of German Foreign Minister Neurath and discuss the Manchurian issue with him. He then went to Hamburg to visit the commercial port. When Matsuoka was in Berlin, he gave a speech to the German heavy industry newspaper "Daily Mann Report," stating that his trip to Moscow was of a private nature, but he had free talks with key Soviet Russian government officials in order to improve relations between Japan and Russia. Matsuoka also said that at this moment, Japanese public opinion is more favorable towards Soviet Russia and that he hopes the import of Japanese goods into Russia can continue to increase. He then spoke about the establishment of the "New Manchurian Nation," saying that Japan should take various measures to support it. When a reporter from the newspaper asked Matsuoka whether "Manchukuo" would grant Japan preferential tariff rates, Matsuoka replied that he did not know about "Manchukuo's" intention in this regard. He also stated that "Manchukuo" should grant equal rights to the powers in accordance with the open-door principle. Matsuoka did not confirm the rumor that "Manchukuo" would raise funds in Japan. As for the commercial situation in Manchuria, Matsuoka said that he was satisfied, and that the value of "Manchukuo" currency in Shanghai was higher than that of Chinese silver dollars. Speaking of the "Manchukuo" army, Matsuoka said that this army currently has 100,000 personnel and is being trained by a large number of Japanese instructors. As for Japan's attitude towards the Lytton Report, there is no need to mention it at this moment. He believes that if a country signs an agreement with another country and recognizes its independence, the League of Nations should not make any decisions or interfere.

Mussolini Reviews Defense Forces

Reuters, Rome, 11th—Italian Prime Minister Mussolini today reviewed a nine-regiment parade of the Rome defense forces as part of the celebrations for the Italian Emperor's birthday. Hundreds of carrier pigeons were released in the parade ground, first flying in a circle in the sky, and then flying away in formation. Italian Air Minister Balbo, who previously led many aircraft to South America, is scheduled to personally lead an air force on a round-trip flight across the Atlantic again next summer.

Japanese Expand Market Through Illegitimate Means

Reuters, London, 11th—Recently, there have been repeated reports that Japanese people are using English trademarks and the names of British merchants to harm British trade. The Parliamentary Secretary of the Board of Trade, Mr. Runciman, also mentioned the Japanese infringement of human commerce during a debate on economic events in the House of Commons today. It is said that the Japanese only entered the British rubber shoe market last year, but within a year, Japan has become the largest supplier of this kind of commodity. The impact of Japan's active exports on world trade and the efforts of the Japanese to expand their market by adopting means that we consider unfair competition can be seen from this.

Reuters, London, 11th—The House of Commons has approved an order to increase import tariffs on Japanese rubber shoes and other items. According to the original tariff, the tax was 20% ad valorem. From now on, rubber shoes will be subject to an additional tax of three to five pence per pair.

500,000 Unemployed in Japan

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 12th—According to a survey by the Social Affairs Bureau of the Ministry of Home Affairs, as of July 1st, the number of unemployed people nationwide was 500,901. This is higher than the average of 470,000 to 480,000 in the past five years and is the highest record since the survey began in 1925.

Important News

Record of Fierce Battles by Righteous Armies

Righteous Flags Everywhere in Southern Liaoning and Andong

Killing Sounds Resound in Liaoyang and Yixian

Tianjin Correspondence: Righteous armies in various parts of Northeast China have sprung up like mushrooms. Although they are in the midst of icy and snowy conditions, they continue to fight fiercely with the enemy. There are many tragic acts among them. Unfortunately, due to traffic obstruction and the lack of propaganda personnel, many have been buried. Here are a few reports of the righteous armies obtained from a certain source, which are unknown to people within the Pass. They are recorded below because the heroic act of fighting for the survival of the nation should not be erased.

Report from Cao Zhen, commander of the 30th Division of the Northeast People's National Salvation Army, and Wei Yuntai, deputy commander: 1. In September, they received military supplies such as bullets, sabers, and bombs in Tianjin. After all kinds of dangers and hardships, they safely transported them to their destination in southern Liaoning on September 24th. They immediately distributed them to various regiments and battalions to step up their work. They then received a secret order from Chief Supervisor Zhu Jiqing, instructing them on combat tactics. On October 2nd, they ordered Regiment Commander Wang Kuiyi to lead his unit to attack Gushan. They fought against the Japanese garrison and the local Datong team at Jiudaogou. The enemy had a total force of about 1,000 people, with five aircraft supporting them in the air. Our army, with 800 men, bravely fought the enemy in a bloody battle all day long. Our Regiment Commander Wang took the lead and bravely moved forward. Due to the enemy's fierce artillery fire, he was seriously injured. He still shouted to advance and kill the enemy. He died smiling for his country due to his serious injuries and lack of medical treatment. The army retreated to Huangtukang due to the loss of its commanding officer and sent a telegram requesting reinforcements. In this battle, more than 30 enemies were killed and many were injured. Our army suffered more than 20 officers and soldiers killed and 14 wounded due to enemy aircraft bombing. After receiving the report, Zhen and others immediately led their troops and the Big Sword Squad to reinforce and fought a major battle with the Japanese soldiers at Huangtukang. Japanese aircraft came to assist again. Our soldiers used water-cooled Maxim guns to shoot them down while lying down. The enemy was surrounded by us and broke through, retreating to Zhuanghe. This battle was fierce for up to eleven hours. More than 50 enemies were killed, 35 rifles, more than 2,000 bullets, two mule carts, and many military supplies were seized. Nine soldiers of our army were killed and 14 wounded. Nearby villages were bombed by Japanese aircraft, and the tragic situation was unbearable to witness. However, the people admired Chief Supervisor Zhu's determination to save the country, and although they suffered sacrifices, they had no complaints. The weather here is getting colder, and all officers and soldiers do not have cotton clothes or fur coats. In addition, nine out of ten households in the countryside are empty, and supplies are difficult to obtain. They urgently need considerable assistance. 2. Since the September 18th Incident, the local military and political power in Liaoning and Andong counties has been controlled by Li Shoushan, who was appointed by Japan as the overseas commander. He recruited bandits and ruffians and had two brigades of troops. Japan supplied them with guns, artillery, and ammunition. They were very well-equipped and repeatedly fought with the army, massacring our compatriots. It cannot be overstated. The Japanese Emperor commended Li for being able to kill Chinese people and specially awarded him a precious sword as encouragement. Li has become more powerful as he recognizes the enemy as his father. Last month (October) on the 20th, he personally led a mixed brigade, together with a Japanese garrison regiment, to Dagushan and attacked our army. Our side immediately sent Regiment Commander Xu Huchen to lead his entire regiment to resist. They fought fiercely at Qingduizi all day long. Both sides suffered casualties. Zhen led his troops to assist at dawn on the 21st, and the morale was greatly boosted. Li Shoushan's younger brother, Battalion Commander Li (Model Battalion, consisting of four infantry companies, one machine gun company, and one mortar company), was killed on the spot, along with more than 50 other officers and soldiers and more than 10 Japanese soldiers. More than 20 were injured, and 23 rifles, more than 50 mules and horses, and many bullets and military supplies were captured. The Japanese and their puppet troops immediately collapsed. Our army was pursuing, originally intending to wipe them out in one fell swoop, but Japanese aircraft arrived and bombed our army. In order to preserve our strength, we had to order a retreat, and temporarily stationed at □□gou □□gou. Because this place is a convenient route to Tongxiuman, the liaison between the Japanese and puppet troops in Zhuanghe and Xiuyan was cut off. Liu, the county magistrate of Xiuyan and commander of the militia regiment, sent a representative to contact our army on the 24th to implement a revolt. They were submitted to Chief Supervisor Zhu and appointed as commander of the 36th Route of the National Salvation Army. Deng Houmei, the county magistrate of Fengcheng, also led his troops west to cooperate with us. Even more people from nearby villages brought their guns to join us, no less than 100,000 people, and the military might was greatly boosted. Li led the remnants to retreat to Dagushan. Our army surrounded Dagushan in three routes on the 28th, waiting for them to run out of food and ammunition, and they would collapse on their own. It is expected that the elimination of Li will make it easier to recover the counties in southern Liaoning.

Continued Important News

Report from a special correspondent in the Liaoshen area □□□: 1. Nanyu District of Liaoyang was completely recovered by Zhang Huamin, commander of the 2nd Regiment of the Independent 5th Division of our army. The entire armed population of the five districts united to resist Japan. The strength and power of our army are growing stronger day by day. It is easy to attack and defend, relying on the mountains and rivers. The Japanese army is quite anxious. Ten days ago (mid-October), the Japanese sent more than 500 troops to attack, but they were surrounded by our army, and more than 20 enemies were killed, and seven vehicles of baggage were seized. The remnants fled in a panic and were surrounded by our friendly forces, and more than half were annihilated, with few surviving. 2. Since my work began, in addition to guiding the formation of various units to actively attack the enemy at any time, I have also sent many comrades to various places to carry out activities. Previously, Mr. □□□ used the name of an education inspector to go to the fourth and fifth districts to promote resistance against Japan, and then led more than 2,000 armed people to rise up against Japan. 3. Now, the righteous armies in the Liaoshen area have no place to hide because the green gauze curtains have fallen, and they are often bombed by Japanese aircraft. Except for a few who surrendered to the enemy due to environmental constraints, the majority regarded surrendering to the enemy as a great shame and contacted our army to cooperate. Although our army has a safe and solid base, it is difficult to obtain salaries and weapons, and we urgently hope that the headquarters will provide sufficient assistance. Gao Pengzhen, the second commander of the National Salvation Army, reported on the order of Zhu to lead troops to attack Yixian: 1. On September 29th, he led seven cavalry companies, departed from Heishan County □□. At 6:00 PM on the same day, he arrived at Beixiagouzi, Beizhen County (60 Chinese miles from the county seat) and camped. At dawn the next day, just as he was preparing to move forward, Dezi, Shuangshan, and Xinlai, leaders of the puppet Nationalist Corps of Beizhen, led more than 2,000 infantry militia to surround us. Fortunately, our army was prepared early and was able to respond calmly. After fierce fighting until noon, the enemy side killed a squad leader and 17 militiamen, and many were injured. Our side only injured three people and killed three horses. The enemy side deceived our isolated army and was trapped, and at 6:00 PM, they carried out a close-range encirclement. Peng saw that the time had come to dusk, and the opportunity could not be missed, so he selected strong and brave men with handguns to form a commando team, and separately sent the sixth company as a left flank to attack the Dashanzhu Village in the left front, and sent the seventh company as a right flank, and detoured to the enemy's rear to disrupt, in order to cover our army's safe retreat. At 10:00 PM, all retreated to Xiaonanshan to reorganize and rest. Three of our soldiers were injured and one horse was killed. The number of enemy deaths and injuries is unknown. At 12:00 PM, they marched towards Laoye Ridge. At 8:00 AM on October 1st, they arrived at Minjia Dianzi (the village originally had the Fa Zi unit of the People's National Salvation Army). They rested at Xiaobaitun, a few miles away from the village. At 9:20, Shan, the director of the Beizhen Puppet Public Security Bureau, led 500 public security teams, two field guns, and received orders from the Japanese army to attack from the left rear. Because our cavalry had difficulty fighting in the mountains, all of them immediately retreated to Minjia Dianzi, occupied the position, and confronted the enemy. The Fa Zi unit of the National Salvation Army in the village also had 200 people and 35 Big Sword Squads who joined the battle, and the morale was boosted. About half an hour later, our army occupied Xiaobaitun and killed a puppet public security director, a puppet battalion commander, and two squadron leaders in the Dayuan of West Street, and killed 25 public security teams. The exact number of injured is unknown. Our Big Sword Squad seized 15 large and small guns and one cannon (which was damaged). At 3:00 PM, the Japanese army used aircraft to bomb from the air and snatched the corpses. The enemy did not escape until it was dark. Our army was exhausted after repeated battles and rested temporarily. At 5:00 AM on the 2nd, according to intelligence, the Japanese army ordered Hu Laohuan (Hu Ni Zeng sent his own daughter to marry a Japanese officer) to lead 2,000 Luhuahui to attack from Zhengnanshan. Our army immediately selected 350 commando troops, together with 2,000 Fa Zi troops and 35 Big Sword Squads, to launch a fierce attack and occupy Nanshan. Taking advantage of the victory, they pursued for 50 miles, to the north of Goubangzi for more than ten miles. The remnants were supported by the Japanese army, and our army retreated back to Minjia Dianzi. In this battle, 13 enemies were killed and the injured are unknown. One of our men died, one gun was lost, and one horse was lost. At 5:00 AM on the 4th, according to espionage, the Japanese army sent two companies from Goubangzi, one company from Beizhen, one aircraft, two cannons, 15 cars, two tank cars, and the entire county public security team to surround us, blocking the mountain passes. Peng then led the 3rd, 4th, 5th, and 7th companies to retreat to the Yijieshimenzizi. The 1st, 2nd, and 6th companies were surrounded by the Japanese army and trapped in the valley. Three assaults were unsuccessful. In this battle, 19 enemy officers and soldiers were killed and one gun was obtained. Eighteen of our men were killed, 39 were injured, 31 guns were lost, and 161 horses were killed. Our army was hit hard, and ammunition and supplies were exhausted. The future is still unknown. They had no choice but to reorganize the team and detour to the back of Heishan that night at 8:00 PM, etc. (November 10th)

Legislative Yuan Passes

Shanghai Disaster Area Reconstruction Public Bonds

The Legislative Yuan's 210th meeting on the 12th passed the Shanghai Disaster Area Reconstruction Public Bonds Regulations. The original text is as follows: Article 1: In order to reorganize roads, bridges, ditches, and carry out other post-disaster construction and relief matters in the disaster area of Shanghai, the Shanghai Municipal Government issues public bonds of 6 million yuan, named Shanghai Disaster Area Reconstruction Public Bonds. Article 2: The interest rate of this public bond is set at 7% per annum. Article 3: This public bond will be issued in November of the 21st year of the Republic of China. Article 4: This public bond is actually received at 80% of the face value. Article 5: The interest and principal of this public bond will be paid at the end of April and the end of October each year. Article 6: Starting from April of the 22nd year of the Republic of China, this public bond will be repaid in installments over 20 years by lottery. The total amount of each lottery will be repaid in accordance with the existing redemption and interest payment table until the end of October of the 41st year of the Republic of China, and all principal and interest will be paid off. The aforementioned lottery will be held on April 5th and October 5th each year, and the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Audit will send personnel to supervise. Article 7: The winning bond tickets of this public bond have a period of six years to collect payment, and the due interest coupons have a period of three years to collect payment, and no further payment will be made after the expiration. Article 8: This public bond is designated by the Shanghai Municipal Government to be used as a redemption and interest payment fund for the income from the wharf donation in this city, and shall deposit the amount specified in the redemption and interest payment table in designated banks of the fund management committee in installments for payment of due principal and interest. The aforementioned fund management committee shall be organized by one person each from the Ministry of Finance and the Shanghai Municipal Government, and one representative each from the Shanghai Banking Association, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, and the banks underwriting this public bond. Article 9: The face value of this public bond is set at 1,000 yuan and 100 yuan. Article 10: This public bond is in unregistered form. Article 11: This public bond can be freely mortgaged and traded, and can be used as a guarantee deposit or collateral for official duties in this city, and as a fund or reserve for public organizations and institutions in this city. Its due principal and interest coupons can be used to pay taxes and fees in this city. Article 20: The redemption and interest payment matters of this public bond shall be handled by the banks entrusted by the fund management committee. Article 13: Those who forge this public bond ticket and damage its credit shall be punished by the judicial organ according to law. Article 14: This regulation shall be implemented from the date of promulgation.

Guizhou Army's Joint Suppression of Communist Bandits in Suichuan

Li Zhenqiu Reports on Bandit Suppression Situation Upon Returning to Guizhou

Southern Jiangxi is Peaceful, Only Anyuan Still Has Bandit Traces

Guangzhou Correspondence: The Southern Jiangxi Defense Army has recently stepped up its guard on the Southern Jiangxi defense line, because the eastern and western Guizhou have simultaneously launched a large-scale crackdown on communists. Yu Hanmou, the commander of the 1st Army of Guizhou, has dispatched the Zhao Lian unit of the 1st Training Regiment of the army to be responsible for guerrilla warfare in the Nankang area to clear out the remaining bandits in the area and to facilitate timely information from the front. He ordered the Ganzhou Camp to plan to set up relay posts in the counties of Ganzhou, Nankang, Shangyou, Chongyi, and Xinfeng. Once the budget is approved, it can be established. Li Zhenqiu, the commander of the 1st Division of the 1st Army stationed in Jiangxi, returned to Guizhou by plane on the 4th. It is said that the whereabouts of the communist bandits in Jiangxi Province are elusive, and the main force is unknown. Our army has no choice but to take a step-by-step approach and respond to the situation as it arises. The bandits who recently disturbed Suichuan were the remnants of Lin Biao's bandit gang in Dawangdong. Because the Dawangdong bandit's nest was broken by our army last month, Lin Biao's bandits scattered to Zuoyingqian. For strategic reasons, our army did not send troops to pursue, so the remnants of Lin Biao continued to gather in Tanggang Suichuan and united with the Xintang local communists, gathering more than 5,000 people and about 2,000 guns, and attacked the Central Army's 28th Division stationed in Suichuan County. At that time, only a small part of the 28th Division was stationed in the city, and due to the disparity in numbers, they were forced to withdraw. Later, when our army heard the news, they sent ten battalions of troops to Shangyou and assisted in the suppression of bandits in Xintang. The Zhou Division of the Central Army also attacked from Wanan and finally defeated the Suichuan bandit. The bandits fled in two routes, one route fled back to Xintang along the original route, and the other route dispersed to eastern Hunan. Suichuan is still guarded by the Central Army, and there are no more bandit traces in the vicinity. As for the area below Ganzhou, our army has set up defenses at every point and formed a mutual defense with the troops stationed in Sannan. The Sannan area is currently stationed by the 4th Division of the 2nd Army and the Wang Division of the Guizhou Army. Local communists have been cleared out from Xinfeng to Longnan, but in Anyuan, there are still several thousand Red Guards belonging to the bandits, who appear from time to time. However, this unit is not the main force of the Red Bandits, and its combat effectiveness is weak and not enough to worry about. (November 7th)

Large-Scale Farm to be Established in Northern Jiangsu

Name to be the Trust Group Farm

Plan to Borrow 100 Million Yuan of Foreign Capital to Operate

Nantong Correspondence: In order to reclaim the coastal wasteland in northern Jiangsu, the Jiangsu Provincial Government has designated the northern Jiangsu reclamation zone, starting from Dongtai Jiaoxie, passing through Yancheng Funing, and ending at Chenjiagang in Lianshui, as a reclamation special zone, and designated the Jiangsu Provincial Security Team to protect the reclamation area and stationed at appropriate locations, and organized a reclamation committee to measure official and private land and plan the progress. Now, He Yingqin, Gu Zhutong, Yao Shiyong, Rong Zongjing, Chen Yi, He Yushu, Dong Xiujia, Li Mingyang, Miao Bin, Zhang Xiaoruo, Leng Yu, Wu Zhaozeng, and other 12 people have launched the establishment of the Northern Jiangsu Coastal Trust Group Farm to undertake the production of all products in the reclamation special zone, as follows: 1. This farm is a group reclamation farm that is entrusted by various farmers and reclamation companies in the Northern Jiangsu Reclamation Special Zone. With the approval of the Central Government through the Jiangsu Provincial Government, it is specifically permitted to manage, invest, and operate all farmland, land property, water conservancy projects, and all production enterprises in the special zone. 2. This farm shall have several trustees who shall be responsible for managing all farmland, land property, raising capital, and operating production in the reclamation special zone. Its purpose and power are entirely to seek the interests of the trust shareholders. 3. All people or companies in the reclamation special zone who hold barren and reclaimed land with undetermined property rights shall be natural shareholders of this farm. The farm shall issue land trust shares according to the land price stipulated by the government. 4. All people or companies in the reclamation special zone who hold determined property rights may join this farm or not, as they see fit. Those who join shall be treated the same as natural shareholders. Those who do not join shall not hinder the unified water conservancy projects in the special zone, and may be consulted for regional adjustments when needed by this farm. 5. The trustees have full power to handle all affairs of this farm. Unless there is corruption or damage to this farm, the trust shareholders shall not interfere. 6. Trust shareholders shall not demand the apportionment of land unless this farm cannot invest in operation and group production. 7. Trust shares are denominated in units of 100 yuan, and the annual dividend is set at 7%. 8. This farm shall have one general manager and two deputy managers, who shall be mutually elected from among the trustees. It is heard that the sponsors have also drafted a five-year production plan budget, planning to borrow 100 million yuan of foreign capital within five years, all at an annual interest rate of 6%, and repay the loan in installments from the sixth to the tenth year.

▲ Entertainment Fair for the Northeastern Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army. Various circles in this county, in view of the loyalty and bravery of the Northeastern Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army and the widespread suffering in the disaster areas, planned to provide assistance. ▲ The Case of the Experimental School Site. The Provincial Office ordered a joint measurement. The Songjiang Girls' Middle School Experimental Elementary School reported that it needed twenty-eight mu of land, including a bit more, at the old Songjiang Almshouse located near Guanghua Temple, next to the motor road. The application was submitted by the Shatin Bureau and approved by the Finance Department. Later, Zhang Jiecai also applied for land in the same area, alleging that the school had destroyed boundary markers and was using civilian land as school grounds, etc., and filed a complaint with the Finance Department. The Finance Department ordered the County Government to reply as to who had encroached on the land. It should be clarified by a joint measurement based on the map approved by the Ministry. The Training Department also issued an order to the Official Property Bureau, scheduling a joint measurement with the county according to the map. Subsequently, the Education Department also stated that since the case involved disputes between school property and civilian land, it should be resolved as soon as possible. The Finance Department sent Shen Chao and the Education Department sent Xue Zhenling as representatives to Songjiang, notifying all parties involved to go to the site for a joint measurement at 1 p.m. today. The resolution of the matter depends entirely on the outcome of the joint measurement.

Suzhou

The Dang Kou Ferry Was Robbed Mid-Journey. The China Merchants Bureau's inland ferry, which was heading from Suzhou to Dang Kou, was carrying over a hundred passengers on the morning of the 12th. At 8 a.m., it departed from Dang Kou for Suzhou. When it reached the Weijing Tang area, it was suddenly attacked by a bandit ship carrying six bandits dressed in yellow uniforms and armed with box cannons. The robbery lasted half an hour, during which five passengers were robbed, losing approximately five to six hundred yuan.

Nanhui

The County Government Executes Two Robbers. On the night of June 6th this year, the homes of Shen Nianchun and Shen Yousheng in Shenjiazhai near Hangtou Town in this county were suddenly robbed by more than twenty bandits armed with weapons, who stole silver dollars, clothing, and other items. That night, two robbers, Wang San and Zhao Xiaosizi, were intercepted by the Yangsi Bridge Public Security Branch of Shanghai County in Zhoujiadu, and the stolen goods were recovered. After preliminary interrogation by the station, the robbers confessed to the robbery and admitted to carrying the stolen goods in an attempt to escape. They were immediately handed over to the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau for investigation. Upon hearing the news, the County Government prepared a document to bring them back. After a clear confession was obtained, they were sentenced to death. The sentence was approved by the Provincial Government. At 9 a.m. yesterday, the two criminals were brought out of prison, their identities were verified, and they were escorted to the execution ground outside the South Gate for execution by firing squad.

Tan Yigui, the County Magistrate of Changshu, convened the Second County Administrative Conference at the Yinzhi Hall of the First District Office from November 7th to 9th. The opening ceremony was held on the morning of the 7th, and a vice-chairman was elected (Pang Diancai was elected with the most votes). Draft proposals were discussed. Wuxi

Cars Forced to Stop Operating. The northern section of the Xicheng Road (towards Jiangyin) is uneven and unsafe for vehicles. The Long-Distance Bus Company is responsible for the repairs, and the expenses are deducted from the road maintenance donation. During the road repair period, long-distance buses reduced the number of runs, and ordinary cars were all suspended. Small car companies believe that their livelihood has been cut off and have repeatedly requested a change of plan, but to no avail. Therefore, they continued to operate. At 5 p.m. the day before yesterday, three small cars, including No. 1218, etc., went from Xi to Cheng and paid one yuan each for road maintenance donations. Unexpectedly, when they drove to the Tangtou Bridge near Chenjing, the manager of the Long-Distance Company in Cheng, Zheng Zhixian, ordered the petition police to pry off the magnetic license plates from the cars and prohibit them from going to Cheng. They had to turn back. At 6 a.m. yesterday, a small car, No. 133, etc., paid the road maintenance donation and obtained a driving license in Xi. At about 10 a.m., a small car, No. 123, etc., paid the donation and opened the ticket in Cheng. Unexpectedly, all subsequent cars were prevented from driving by the Long-Distance Company, which aroused public outrage. At 3 p.m., all the small cars drove to the Yangxiang area near the Yanqiao area of Xijing and blocked the long-distance buses from driving. Zhang Xin and others, the head of the 13th Public Security Branch in that area, received the report and led the police to the scene to persuade the drivers, and then persuaded the cars to drive into the city. They formally submitted a request for relief. Long-distance buses were also able to drive into the city, but it was already around 5 o'clock. This morning (the 12th) at 10 a.m., Xiao Zicai, the director of the County Construction Bureau, summoned representatives of the small car companies to the bureau to persuade them to request assistance in accordance with the law and not to cause more accidents. The representatives then left and telegraphed the Provincial Party Department, the Provincial Government, the Construction Department, and the Minister of Civil Affairs on the same day to request assistance.

▲ Conference on Promoting Public Warehouses in Various Counties. The Wuxi County Chamber of Commerce, entrusted by the Jiangsu-Shanghai Public Food Regulation Association in accordance with the resolution of the first committee meeting on October 29, specially sent letters to the Wujin, Jiangyin, Yixing, and Liyang County Chambers of Commerce, inviting representatives of relevant organizations in accordance with Article 2 of the established regulations to meet in Xi the day before yesterday (the 11th) afternoon. Representatives from the Wujin, Jiangyin, and Wuxi County Chambers of Commerce, as well as the Farmers Bank and the Food Administration Committee, including Lin Junbao, Wu Shuying, Gu Shuzhi, and Qian Sunji, and more than 20 others attended the meeting. Hua Yinchun, instructor of the Industry Department, Chen County Magistrate, and Xu Yongji, executive member of the County Party Department, were invited to attend for guidance. Qian Sunqing was elected chairman to report on the progress of the two meetings in Xi and Zhen, as well as the two committee meetings in Zhen and Shanghai, and to discuss the promotion of rural public warehouses. As a result of the discussion, under the principle of regulating rice prices and preserving agricultural products, the following was decided: 1. Regarding the regulation of rice prices, the attending representatives should jointly urge the government to issue a clear order as soon as possible on the two items of opening the rice ban and collecting import and export taxes on foreign rice, so as to provide relief and avoid falling prices. 2. Regarding rural public warehouses, in accordance with Article 3 of the established implementation measures, the Farmers Bank shall be responsible for contacting Jiangyin and Wuxi, and Yili and Wujin, according to the original regional divisions of the bank and the convenience of the facts, and the attending representatives shall actively cooperate with the local party and government public groups at any time to ensure safety and avoid difficulties. After the above discussions were completed, it was near dusk, and the meeting was adjourned. It was also heard that the Suzhou Chamber of Commerce had invited the Kunshan and Wujiang County Chambers of Commerce, Farmers Bank, and relevant organizations to meet in Su on the 14th to discuss the progress together.

▲ Five-Year Engineering Plan of the Reclamation Corps. The Jiangsu Provincial Reclamation Corps is implementing reclamation of the coastal wasteland in northern Jiangsu, implementing a five-year engineering plan. 1. Water conservancy project, A. The construction of the new canal requires a total of 16.2 million cubic meters of earthwork, costing 8.1 million yuan. Using machinery, it can be completed within one year. B. The coastal river dikes are about 400 li long. In addition to using the existing sea dikes, the new dikes are less than 120 li. The total cost of construction is 3.51 million yuan. C. Gates, the reclamation area needs to build six large gates, costing a total of 5.05 million yuan. D. Bridges, 40 new canals and 560 seaports, cost a total of 1.88 million yuan. E. Dredging fee of 714,510 yuan. F. Equipment fee of 2 million yuan. G. Planting vegetation on all uncultivated barren land in the area requires 4 million yuan. The total cost of the above water conservancy project is 25,254,510 yuan. After the completion of this project, the entire area can be free from drought and flood, and the salinity of the land can be gradually reduced, and results will be achieved within five years. 2. Production plan, within five years, the production bank operated with foreign capital can accumulate 10 million yuan, which is enough to guarantee debts and more. From the sixth year to the tenth year, the loans can be repaid in installments.

Changzhou

Yicheng Cloth Factory Found to Have Smuggled Enemy Machinery. Xu Zhenxiang and Xu Runxiang, the persons in charge of the Yicheng Cloth Factory in Mahangqiao, Wuyi County, secretly imported enemy goods such as steel thorns and springs in Shanghai, and were found and punished by the Anti-Japanese Association. Recently, the Anti-Japanese Association received a confidential letter reporting that the factory had secretly imported a large number of enemy machines. Inspectors Huang Yisun and others were dispatched to investigate, and cloth machines were indeed found, with the words "Toyota-style Cloth Machine Co., Ltd." on them. They were filed off and replaced with a copper plate from the Shanghai Jinchang Iron Factory to cover up the fact. Manager Xu Zhenxiang, knowing that things were not going well, took the opportunity to escape. A total of 66 enemy machines were inventoried in the entire factory, and the gantry supports were dismantled and brought back that night to await disposal.

A Fire in the Second District Destroyed Twenty-One Homes. ▲ Record of Robberies and Kidnappings. Anqing

The Provincial Government Sent Personnel to Investigate the Xiuning Riot Case. The Anhui Civil Affairs Department recently received a report from Wang Mingyi, the County Magistrate of Xiuning, stating that more than a thousand rioters in the county were restless and planning to join forces with the county government of Qi County to encircle and suppress them. They immediately ordered proper handling and reporting. After receiving the order, the County Magistrate led the police force to encircle and suppress them. Later, the Section Chief of the County Government and the Chief of the Public Security Bureau sent telegrams one after another, saying that the police force brought by County Magistrate Wang had now returned, and the whereabouts of the County Magistrate were unknown. Yesterday, the Civil Affairs Department received two telegrams from Wang Shugong, the Chief County Magistrate of Qi County in the Tenth District, on the 8th and 9th, stating that they had been ordered to send a team to accompany County Magistrate Wang to Huangjian Village to investigate the case of a dispute between the Cheng and Huang families over the Damaiwu mountain farm, in which they accused each other of causing trouble. A small number of stubborn people took risks because the mountain farm was taken away. County Magistrate Wang died from his injuries. According to the telegrams sent by He Shouren, the Section Chief of Xiuning County, and Li Ruinian, the Chief of the Public Security Bureau of Tunxi, the matter was of great importance, and the Provincial Government should send senior officials to lead a team to investigate and arrest the criminals together with the counties of Xi and Qi, severely punish them, investigate the truth of the trouble, and resolve all pending cases. The deceased County Magistrate Wang Mingyi died from injuries sustained in the line of duty, and should be given preferential treatment. After receiving the telegram, the Civil Affairs Department immediately submitted the matter to the Provincial Government's Talk Conference yesterday (the 11th) and decided to send Commissioner Jiang Tonghou to supervise the Administrative Inspector of the district to investigate the matter severely, and the Security Office of the Civil Affairs Department should send personnel to assist in the handling. The deceased County Magistrate Wang Mingyi died a tragic death, and 1,000 yuan was allocated for funeral expenses in advance, and the Civil Affairs Department should investigate the pension system and give preferential treatment.
