Strong Winds at Songkou Hinder Navigation

Ningbo-bound Vessel Returns to Shanghai

Since the 11th, a hurricane occurred in Little Luzon, moving north, affecting the South China Sea area. Many sea vessels were hit by the wind. The Taikoo Company's New Beijing vessel, heading to Ningbo on Friday, sailed out of Wusong on the same day. When it reached the sea area of Daqishan, the wind became stronger, and the navigation was dangerous. In order to ensure the safety of the voyage, the shipowner temporarily suspended the voyage. Then, because the wind was not calming down, it was decided to return to Shanghai. It arrived at Wusong at about 10:00 PM that night. Because it was late at night, it could not enter the port and was changed to Shanghai yesterday morning. All passengers on board were refunded their tickets and disembarked. The vessel is scheduled to depart on Monday.

▲ Wind Heading North

According to a report from the Xujiahui Observatory yesterday, there is still a hurricane east of Little Luzon, heading north. It has reached the vicinity of Shandong. There are northwest and northeast winds along the Chinese coast. There will continue to be hurricanes between Taiwan and Luzon, blowing northeast. The new Ningbo-Shaoxing vessel, which was sheltering from the wind outside Wusong, did not return yesterday and had already departed for Ningbo in the morning.

Shanghai University Bus and

Tram Collide in Tragic Accident

Bus Driver Driving Too Fast

Tram Speed Also Too Fast

Worker Thrown to Death After Collision

Four Students Injured

Shanghai University Bus Smashed to Pieces

Yesterday at 9:45 AM, a bus and a tram collided at the intersection of Yangshupu and Shengs Road, causing casualties. The details are as follows:

▲ Two Vehicles Collide

Yesterday was the Premier's Memorial Day, and all schools in the city were closed. Shanghai University of Shanghai also closed as usual. Therefore, a group of students at the school took the school's own No. 16114 bus at about 9:00 AM to go out. Because the driver saw that this place was quiet, he drove at full speed. When it reached the intersection of Broadway and Huasheng Road near the Ewo factory, the driver still did not slow down. At this time, a No. 73, 8th Route tram from the 16th Pu to Yangshupu was speeding from west to east. The bus driver originally thought of crossing over, but when he saw that the tram was too late, he quickly turned the car. At the same time, the tram driver braked seeing the car coming out sideways, and was also too late to brake. Therefore, the tram crashed into the bus.

▲ Worker Dies Tragically

With a loud bang, the bus was smashed to pieces, and the windows of the tram were shattered. A worker-like person standing on the front platform of the tram could not dodge when the two vehicles collided and was thrown out of the vehicle. His abdomen was broken, and his intestines flowed out. He died on the spot. The students in the bus were seriously injured when the vehicle overturned. They were groaning in the car. Fortunately, the workers and residents of the nearby Ewo Company and other factories heard the alarm and rushed to the scene of the accident to rescue the injured from the vehicle. At the same time, they reported to the police.

▲ Condition of the Injured

The police notified the Yangshupu Fire Brigade to send an ambulance. On one hand, Chinese and foreign detectives were dispatched to rush to the scene and send the injured to Tongren Hospital for treatment. The body of a worker who had died by the road was also sent to the Forensic Examination Office on Filun Road for examination. Then, the dimensions of the intersection where the accident occurred were surveyed. On one hand, the destroyed bus was transported away, and the blood stains on the ground were washed away. The tram driver was immediately taken to the police station for questioning. All passengers on the tram, except for Wen Xichang and Cheng Wenda, whose hands and feet were seriously injured and were hospitalized, were slightly injured, so they were discharged from the hospital after being bandaged by the hospital. The students in the bus who were sent to Tongren Hospital due to injuries were Dai Jiaju, Zhu Dezhou, Li Haichun, and Xu Huandi. Among them, Dai and Zhu were slightly injured and were discharged from the hospital. The other two are still under treatment. The police are investigating the family members of the worker-like person to identify them.

According to Shanghai University news, at 9:00 AM yesterday, several students from Shanghai University of Shanghai asked for leave to take the public bus prepared by a private individual in the school to the city. The car arrived in Yangshupu. On the way, the vehicles were crowded and suddenly collided with a 9-way tram. Four students, Li Ruchun, Xu Huandi, Lu Zhongyu, and Chen Qi, were injured and sent to Tongren Hospital. At that time, the school was holding a memorial week. The school's President Liu heard the news and went to the hospital with Dean Fan and Chen Qishan, director of the high school, to visit. It was heard that the injuries of the injured were not very serious.

The City is Preparing to Build Grain Storage Warehouses

Allocating the Remaining Funds from the Former Shangbao Grain Storage Funds

Ordering Bean and Rice Businesses to Prepay 5% Donation

The City Government to Provide Funding for the Deficit

In view of the fact that this year's grain harvest is abundant and grain prices have fallen drastically, which has had a significant impact on the rural economy, and in response to the recent central government order to promote the construction of grain storage warehouses in the city, the City Government, in order to realize the city's warehouse plan and relieve grain prices, first formulated a grain storage warehouse plan by the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau and submitted it to the City Government. The City Government approved it separately and ordered the Social Affairs Bureau to comply with it. The situation and methods of the old Shangbao county grain storage funds are recorded below:

▲ Historical Overview

According to the investigation, the existing funds and assets of the two counties of Shangbao were used up by He Fenglin during the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Qi Lu war in the Republic of China. Therefore, despite the proposal for warehousing, it has not been implemented due to the lack of funds. During the summer and autumn of the 18th and 19th years, rice prices in the city soared, causing extreme panic. Although the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, together with local people, handled Ping Tiao as an emergency measure, it had little effect because the city had no grain storage. Therefore, in November of the 19th year, a fundraising committee was formed for the city's warehousing fund to raise one million yuan of warehousing funds in order to seek a fundamental plan for regulating the people's food. However, fundraising was difficult, and it is still less than 50,000 yuan. During the serious floods in the autumn of last year, in order to prevent the city from becoming unprepared, the Fundraising Committee for the Warehousing Fund petitioned the City Government to order 50,000 bags of foreign rice. However, after the order, due to the sudden outbreak of the incident in the three northeastern provinces, the exchange rate with the British exchange rate lost about 4 yuan, with a loss of 200,000 yuan. In addition to the 50,000 taels that have been paid and another 50,000 yuan offset, the city government has re-filled more than 70,000 yuan, (which is a donation) and still lost 63,442 taels and 4 cents. After the war, the city's finances are no longer what they used to be, but the city government agreed to pay 25,000 taels to settle the outstanding case. There is still a loss of 38,000 taels. 13,400 taels of which are the responsibility of the Warehousing Fund Committee, Gu Xin, to solicit donations from the rice industry. Still missing 25,000 taels, there is no way to make up for it, but at present the foreign rice is full, and the harvest is everywhere, and the rice price continues to plummet, so the city government in order to take emergency measures, will divide the funds from the Liangxian grain accumulation, the city should get 300,000 yuan, and the first year the bean rice industry voluntarily donate to fill in 300,000 yuan as a fund, by the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau together with the land finance bureau to build grain storage warehouses,

▲ Current Methods

The city's grain storage construction method has been approved by the city government, and the Social Affairs Bureau is ordered to handle the following: (1) The Bureau, together with the Land and Finance Bureaus, shall quickly find a way to divide the old grain storage funds of the two counties of Shangbao and hand over the amount that the city should receive, about 300,000 yuan, to the city government for the construction of a new-style warehouse capable of holding 500,000 shi (about one month's grain supply for the city's population. If the 30,000 yuan is not enough, the city government will make up for it.) (2) The Bureau shall quickly discuss with the Bean and Rice Industry and other trade associations to formulate a specific plan for the industry to voluntarily donate a warehouse fund of 5 cents of silver per shi and submit it to the city government for approval. (3) The aforementioned donation fund of 300,000 yuan in the first year shall be raised by the industry first so that the first batch of 37,500 shi of indica rice can be purchased immediately (valued at 8 yuan per shi). (4) For the purchase of the aforementioned rice and grain, the city government may negotiate with the silver and money industry to borrow 600,000 yuan to 1 million yuan in cash so that it can continue to purchase and store it. In this way, the equipment warehouse and the purchase and storage of grain will proceed simultaneously, and there will be no difficulty in the city's economic situation.

French Concession Local Bully Secretly Selling National Territory

Purchased by Toa Dobun Shoin

Hua Dong News reports that the sale of national territory to foreigners violates the ban, and the Party and government authorities have issued repeated warnings. However, recently, Xu Jiyu, a local bully and land guarantor of the 28th Bao 6th Tu in the French Concession, colluded with land vendors Zhu and Ji to privately sell 1.53 mu of land from single household He Dianzhang in the 212th Shanhu of Duanzihui and 0.88 mu of land from number 314, (current property owner He Genfa and He Xiangen, who live at Nantangzi Jing, Hongqiao) to Toa Dobun Shoin through a private contract. The local bully and land vendors dared to take advantage of the anti-Japanese sentiment to profit from greed and violate national law. Therefore, the residents of the area have petitioned the authorities to thoroughly investigate and punish them severely.

The Northern New Bookstore Has Not Yet Been Sealed

The Booksellers' Association Cables Request for Legal Handling

Regarding the case of the "Little Pig Bajie" published by the Northern New Bookstore insulting Islam, the Executive Yuan has already instructed the Shanghai Municipal Government to, together with the court, seal up the Northern New Bookstore. Upon hearing this news, the bookstore immediately announced a temporary closure. At the same time, after receiving the Executive Yuan's instructions, the Municipal Government immediately sent a document to the First Special District Court requesting the execution of the sealing. However, as of last night, the First Special District Court had not yet executed it.

The Booksellers' Association cabled the Central Government yesterday, stating: "To the Nanjing Central Party Headquarters and the Executive Yuan, re: the misunderstanding between Nanhua and the Northern New Bookstore and Muslims caused by the article 'Little Pig Bajie'. The method of handling Nanhua is clearly appropriate. Today's newspaper reported that the Executive Yuan's approval included the words 'the Northern New Bookstore should be sealed immediately,' which is deeply alarming. Firstly, in a country governed by law, no matter what the crime, it should be judged by the court according to law, and there seems to be no reason to seal it immediately. Secondly, since the publisher, editor, and author are being investigated according to law, why must the bookstore be sealed first? Moreover, it is the same crime but different punishment compared to Nanhua. The association has already resolved to order the Northern New Bookstore to publish an apology in the newspaper and send the book to the Shanghai Municipal Government to await legal handling. We earnestly request that the sealing order be revoked immediately in order to comply with the rule of law and maintain commerce. We are filled with trepidation as we await orders."

Representatives of Hebei Muslims Arrive in Shanghai from Beijing

The delegation of Muslim petitioners from Hebei arrived in Shanghai yesterday from Beijing. In addition to the four representatives, Wang Zixin, Wang Mengyang, Liu Boshi, and Ma Ziwen, Tang Kesan, a member of the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission, and Sun Shengwu, the former Director of Finance of Anhui Province, also arrived. When the cars arrived at the North Station, about several hundred Muslims from Shanghai lined up to welcome them with banners that read "Welcome the Petition Representatives from Hebei to Shanghai." They were greeted by Da Pusheng, Ha Decheng, Jin Xusheng, Ha Shaofu, Su Zixiang, and others, and were taken in more than ten cars directly to the Islamic Mosque on Fuyou Road in the city to rest. The Islamic Fellowship hosted a banquet in the temple to welcome the representatives of the petitioners from both the north and south, and invited religious leaders and elders from various places to accompany them. After taking their seats, Su Zixiang, the representative of the Islamic Fellowship, stood up first to deliver a welcoming speech, which briefly stated that it was a great pleasure to welcome the representatives of the petitioners from both the north and south, as well as Mr. Tang Kesan and Mr. Sun Yanwing, and that the northerners and southerners were gathered together. The meaning of the welcome was divided into four points: (1) trust, (2) hard work, (3) success, and (4) cooperation. Then, he recited the welcoming speech. Subsequently, Wang Zixin, Tang Kesan, and Liu Boshi, representatives from the north, delivered speeches thanking them for their welcome. Finally, Da Pusheng, the religious leader, lectured on the 110th chapter of the Quran to encourage his fellow believers, and his words were extremely cautionary. They did not disperse until 11:00 p.m., when they had all enjoyed themselves.

Ningbo Compatriot Association Sends a Letter Requesting

The Municipal Government to Announce the Facts of Wang Xinfu's Case

Business License Certifies Legitimate Merchant

Newspaper Reports of Municipal Government Wanted Case

Therefore, Please Publicly Announce the Case

Wang Xinfu, a native of Ningbo, opened the Huaxing Soap Factory on Yuezhou Road. On the 23rd of last month, a fire broke out in the soap-making oil pot at the factory, leading to a misunderstanding with the fire brigade. He was summoned by the Public Security Bureau of the district. Later, it was rumored that someone accused him of being a traitor, and pointed out that Wang Xinfu was actually the fleeing Wang Du, using a pseudonym. He was escorted to the Ministry of Military Affairs by the Municipal Public Security Bureau for interrogation. His family, feeling that the matter was unjust, appealed to the Ningbo Compatriot Association in Shanghai to redress the grievance, and the factory and business firms there jointly sent a letter guaranteeing that Wang Xinfu was indeed a legitimate merchant. The association, based on the facts, sent a letter to the Municipal Government requesting them to announce the facts of Wang Xinfu's case to clarify the truth. The letter stated: "Respectfully, according to the letter from fellow villager Wang Lichang, (above omitted), my father, Wang Xinfu, was rumored to have been falsely accused of being a traitor, and it was pointed out that my father was the alias of Wang Du. This is a bizarre case of mistaken identity. During the January 28th Incident, our factory was close to the war zone and was forced to close. My father led his family back to his hometown to take refuge. The facts are all there. How can he be called a traitor? Moreover, Wang Du is said to be from Anhui, while my father has lived in Yin County for generations. Such a case of calling a deer a horse and framing someone is unjustifiable. My father is a member of your esteemed association, and we ask you to uphold justice and provide assistance. In addition, fourteen business firms, including Shun Kang Factory, have jointly sent a letter guaranteeing that Wang Xinfu is indeed a merchant and that he has been framed this time, which is indeed a grievance. The association, based on the facts, sent a letter to the Municipal Public Security Bureau requesting them to investigate and release him. Afterwards, we read in the local newspapers of the 11th of this month a news item that the traitor Wang Xinfu was escorted to Beijing for trial. The report stated that the Municipal Government had issued an arrest warrant. My colleagues in the association are deeply suspicious. If Wang Xinfu is a traitor, we should all abandon him and never protect him because of our friendship as fellow villagers. However, the factories and business firms in the neighborhood are all willing to jointly guarantee that Wang Xinfu is indeed a legitimate merchant and are willing to be held jointly liable if there is any falsehood. These factories and business firms all have families and businesses and are so responsible for their guarantees, which proves that Wang Xinfu has absolutely no improper behavior. Is the arrest warrant issued by your government, as reported in the newspaper, true? If it is true that there is an arrest warrant, please publicly announce the facts of the case to clarify the truth and redress the grievance. Therefore, we respectfully request the Mayor to examine and verify the facts and provide a reply. We are deeply grateful."

Reasons for the Public Works Department to Demolish Unregistered Straw Sheds

Regarding the recent demolition of unregistered straw sheds in the eastern district of the concession, various rumors are actually caused by three people who call themselves representatives of the shantytown residents. Two of them are shantytown residents, and the other one is an employee of a yarn factory in Yangshupu and not a shantytown resident. The Public Works Department has always been very considerate of the people living in the straw sheds, but in order to limit the number of these straw sheds, which are detrimental to public health, and to improve the cleanliness of the surrounding environment, the Public Works Department established conditions with the Shantytown Association in July last year to register all existing sheds and prohibit any additional construction in the future. However, after the chaos this spring, many more sheds were added. The Public Works Department, in view of the difficult situation after the war, did not immediately punish them. After the normal state had been restored, the Public Works Department issued a one-month notice in September, ordering the 800 newly built straw sheds to be removed, otherwise they would be demolished. The deadline was already very generous, so after the deadline, people were sent to demolish them, and no one actively opposed it. Now, although the three people who call themselves representatives are making various propaganda, the Shantytown Association knows that these new sheds violate the conditions, and there is no reason to oppose the demolition. Some people may think that the demolition of the straw sheds is only because they are not registered, but they do not know that the original condition was that they were not allowed to be built in the first place.

The Municipal Government Could Not Find the Eight Provinces Righteous Army Preparatory Committee

Said to Be Liu Jue's Claim

It was reported that a certain Liu Jue (alias Meng'an) was staying at Room 811 of the YMCA dormitory. Because he interfered with the business of a store, he was arrested by the French police. At the police station, he claimed to be the secretary of the Chinese consultant of the League of Nations Investigation Team. The police suspected his claims and sent people to investigate the YMCA dormitory. In his room, they searched and removed 17 irrelevant letters, drafts, pawn tickets, etc. The next morning, he was released. Unexpectedly, as soon as Liu regained his freedom, he printed 500 copies of a quick mail telegram in the name of the Preparatory Committee of the Volunteer Allied Army of Eight Southwestern Provinces and distributed them everywhere, and sent them to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs in Nanjing and other places. The telegram stated that the office of the committee was suddenly searched by the armed police of the French Concession on the 3rd, and a number of telegram copies from various provinces, a copy of the English secret code of the Chinese Embassy in Paris, a purchase order for military supplies from the Hong Kong Swiss Foreign Company, a short-term deposit slip from the Shanghai Bank, a deposit certificate in Liu Jue's name from the Northern Continental Bank, and important official documents and seals were all taken away. It was reported that the committee's director, Liu Jue, was under surveillance and shackled. He was released on bail by Gan Jiehou, Zhang Shizhao, and others. According to the report, the Municipal Government immediately sent personnel to investigate the case, since it had never heard of the Volunteer Allied Army of Eight Southwestern Provinces and the case involved the illegal arrest of Chinese citizens in the concession. The investigation revealed that all the claims in Liu's telegram were false. The French police also absolutely denied that he had been shackled. As for the items seized, apart from eleven pawn tickets, three receipts for small sums of money remitted from the Shanghai Bank to Hangzhou, four letters from Zhang Shizhao, and nine bundles of miscellaneous drafts, there was nothing of value. Further investigation at the Shanghai Bank revealed that there was no short-term deposit account in Liu's name. Zhang Shizhao's law office denied that he had posted bail on his behalf, and Gan Jiehou was not in Shanghai at the time. Inquiries at the YMCA dormitory revealed that Liu owed a lot of room and board, barbers fees, etc. The large number of pawn tickets on his bed showed his poverty. The so-called Shanghai office of the Preparatory Committee of the Volunteer Allied Army of Eight Southwestern Provinces was merely Liu's claim. His words and actions seemed to be those of a neurotic.

The Yan Maoyuan Hotel was Suddenly Cut Off from Electricity

The Taxpayers' Association Asks the Public Works Department to Order a Stop to the Action

The Public Concession Chinese Taxpayers Association sent a letter to the General Manager of the Public Works Department regarding the electricity company cutting off the electricity to the Yan Maoyuan Hotel, stating: "Respectfully, according to a letter from the Lao Yan Maoyuan Luji Hotel in Zhongshi, Fuzhou Road, since taking over the business on September 1, 1932, the business has been affected by the war and the business has been in a slump. There are very few customers on the second and third floors, and there are even many nights when no lights are turned on. The electricity consumption downstairs is extremely limited. The monthly fee is clearly marked on the meter. The company sends personnel to verify the meter and issue receipts for payment. There is no allocation arrears or any violation of regulations. However, the company sent someone to the store seven days ago to replace the meter without any prior notice, so we were confused. Unexpectedly, after many days, the company sent someone to the store and ordered us to send someone to the company to negotiate. According to the director, we must pay more than 2,000 taels of silver for electricity bills from September 1, 1931, to the present day within 48 hours, otherwise the electricity will be cut off. The electricity bills are clearly stated on the meter and should be paid monthly. There is no default in payment, which is in accordance with the law and reason. If the electricity is cut off, the business losses will be unimaginable. We respectfully ask your association to uphold justice and strive for our rights to maintain our business. In addition, we have received a letter from the Shanghai Shaoxing Wine Industry Association with the same request. While we were verifying the matter, we received a report from the store stating that the electricity company had cut off the electricity on the afternoon of November 11. Based on this, we have paid the electricity fees according to the meter, which fulfills the responsibility of the user. It is incomprehensible to demand the supplementary payment of electricity fees afterwards. Furthermore, it is improper to ask users to pay supplementary electricity fees based on the unilateral claim of the electricity company without any basis. It is even more outrageous to set a deadline to cut off the electricity. Such actions are close to oppression and cannot be convincing, and will make all users in the concession feel chilled. Everyone is afraid of being coerced into paying supplementary electricity fees under the threat of power outages based on the electricity company's own intentions. Based on the above facts, we hereby send this letter to your office, requesting that you immediately stop the electricity company's power outage and restore the original situation. Please also investigate and determine the basis for demanding that users pay supplementary electricity fees. Sincerely, Shanghai Public Concession Public Works Department."

The Water Supply to Yuanyuli was Suddenly Cut Off

Requesting Fair Mediation

The Real Estate Department of the China Reclamation Bank appealed: "Respectfully, our office has 45 houses in Yuanyuli, Songpan Road, Yangshupu, in the Eastern District, with monthly rentals of approximately 400 yuan. Most of the residents are poor laborers. Since the January 28th Incident, the economy has been sluggish and life has been difficult. However, the British Shanghai Waterworks Company forcibly installed water meters and charged according to the meter at this time. The monthly bill is often around 4,000 gallons, totaling more than 240 yuan, which is almost half of the total rent and more than seven times the rate of 0.075. Our office has been complying with the notice of your association and temporarily paying at the original price before the problem is resolved. However, the company refused to accept the payment and suddenly closed the main pipe at 10:00 a.m. on November 11, cutting off the water supply. The lives of hundreds of residents are at stake. The company's actions are likely to harm more than just our office. We hereby report this to your association and request that you quickly mediate fairly to protect the lives of the people. We are extremely grateful."

Attention to Concession Stores

Installing Wireless Radios

Recently, many stores in the concession have installed wireless radios at the entrance, with the sole purpose of attracting business. However, the sound of the radio often causes passersby and idlers to stop outside the door and listen, causing crowds to gather on the sidewalk, obstructing traffic. Sometimes, these listeners also stand on the road, which really obstructs the traffic of vehicles. The Police Department of the Public Works Department, in view of this, has decided to prohibit such traffic-obstructing behavior. A few days ago, it specifically requested four summons from the Special District Court and summoned the managers of the stores at No. 183, 398, 596, and 688 Xinzha Road on the 9th of this month. After the managers were tried by a certain judge, the police charged them with violating Article 36 of the By-laws of the Public Works Department. Although there was no penalty as a result of the trial, the judge warned the store managers that they must move the wireless radios elsewhere in the future to avoid causing crowds to gather on the sidewalk and obstructing traffic.

Director of the Bureau of Education

Orders Against Arbitrary Intrusion into Homes

Gong Kui, the Superintendent of the Municipal Police Bureau, recently noted that some inspectors from this bureau, without orders, had been arbitrarily entering homes to arrest those involved in flower gambling, leading to the growth of unscrupulous individuals. Some even impersonated public officials, using the guise of arresting flower gamblers to commit fraud. He ordered all inspectors under his command to refrain from arbitrary arrests without specific instructions from him, to prevent abuse and maintain public order. Yesterday, the Director of the Bureau of Education also instructed all bureau staff that the responsibility for apprehending flower gamblers rested solely with the district offices and detective squads, and that they should not arbitrarily search homes. This is of utmost importance.

Guanshengyuan Restaurant's Charity Drive

Today's Entire Revenue Donated to the Northeast Refugee Relief Association

The Guanshengyuan Food Company on Nanjing Road, recently, due to the successive natural disasters and wars in the Northeast provinces, leading to the suffering and displacement of our compatriots, who have lost their livelihoods. At this time of howling winds and bitter cold, the misery of those starving and freezing is unimaginable. In the spirit of human mutual aid, the company is emulating last year's flood relief efforts and donating today's entire revenue from the second-floor restaurant, including the standard 10% service charge and tips for waiters, to the Northeast Refugee Relief Association for aid. Two Hotels Net a Large Group of Robbers

Robbers Leave Restaurant Tickets in Hotel

Detectives Find Clues

Franco-Chinese detectives from the French Concession, acting on information received in the afternoon, discovered a large group of robbers hiding in the Oriental and Far Eastern Hotels at the intersection of Xizang Road and North Sea Road in the Public Concession. They immediately joined forces with detectives from the Laozha Police Station of the Public Concession. They first went to room 453 on the fourth floor of the Oriental Hotel, where they apprehended three robbers. Detectives then disguised themselves as waiters and waited in the room. By late night, they had captured a total of twenty-one members of the gang. Yesterday, they caught three more. Then, they went to the Far Eastern Hotel and apprehended five more robbers. All were taken to the Laozha Police Station to await interrogation. It is reported that the reason for breaking this robber case was that the robbers had robbed a resident with the surname of a certain resident in the French Concession of their belongings. At the time, they robbed silk clothing and exchanged their old clothes, leaving one piece behind at the victim's home. The detectives from the French Concession took it back to the police station, where they found a restaurant ticket for room 453 of the Oriental Hotel and another for a room in the Far Eastern Hotel in the pocket. They went to the addresses and waited to make the arrests. Among these criminals were robbers, kidnappers, and hooligans. All were captured in one fell swoop by the detectives.

Record of the Zhang-Xu Wedding

At 4 PM on the 12th of this month, Mr. Zhang Shenrong, a current commissioner of the Ministry of Railways, and Miss Xu Huiyuan held their wedding ceremony at the Moore Memorial Church on Sanma Road in this city. The wedding was officiated by Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Director of the Finance Department of the Ministry of Railways Chen Yaozu, former Minister to Belgium Wang Jingqi, and Chief Commander Liu Zhilu. Many dignitaries and guests attended, making it a grand affair. The groom, Mr. Zhang, holds a Bachelor of Laws degree from the University of London and studied law in Paris, followed by academic research in Berlin for many years. The bride is the daughter of Mr. Xu Shaoqiu. Mr. Xu followed Sun Yat-sen and Huang Xing in his early years, engaging in revolutionary work, possessing military and political knowledge, and serving in important military and political positions. He devoted himself to the revolution, achieving great accomplishments early in life. His daughter is also well-versed in both Chinese and Western learning and proficient in martial arts. The marriage of these two families, both prominent Cantonese clans, is truly a celebrated event of the time.

Groom Opens Gambling Den, Arrested

Boss Sentenced to Two Months, Gamblers Fined Twenty Yuan Each

Detective Guan Binliang and Western Detective Lin of the Xinzha Police Station, discovered that a stable groom from the Race Club was operating a gambling den at No. 444 Dazhan Road, allowing stable grooms and doormen to gamble inside, profiting from the cut. They secretly arrested the boss, Bei Rongsheng, and gamblers Wang Zhengpeng, Chen Zhengtian, Tang Qingsheng, and others, totaling twenty-two people, mostly stable grooms from the Race Club. They confiscated the Pai Gow tiles, mahjong tiles, wooden tiles, and gambling money and took them to the police station. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the summary court of the First Special District. The police lawyer Qian Xunjiu stated the case, presenting the gambling paraphernalia and money. Judge Huang Risheng questioned each defendant one by one and sentenced the boss, Bei Rongsheng, to two months of imprisonment, and the remaining twenty-one people, including Wang Zhengpeng, were fined twenty yuan each. The gambling paraphernalia and money were confiscated.

Restaurant Employee Conspires Unlawfully after Dismissal

Discussing Robbery in Hotel

Plans Discovered Before Implementation

Zhao A'san, from Wuxi, used to work in a restaurant next to the Grand Theater on Sanma Road. Recently, due to being dismissed for several days, he was short on money and in dire straits, so he came up with the idea that the neighboring liquor and food store did not do so poorly, that there was a chance to rob it. He invited fellow villagers Zhu Fuqian and Zhu Ayin, and Fuqian brought a handgun loaded with five bullets. They went to the Champagne Hotel at 114 Yunnan Road and opened room 34 to discuss how to carry out the robbery. However, the plan was discovered by the Huishi Police Station's Chinese Detective Shang Wu. At 10 PM the previous evening, he brought detectives Wang Youshan and Liu Shaotian, and secretly arrested Zhao and the two Zhus, and confiscated the gun and bullets under the pillow, taking them to the police station. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Second Criminal Court of the First Special District. The police lawyer Wang Yaotang stated the case, saying that the case still needed to be investigated and had not yet been prosecuted, and requested permission to detain them. Judge Wu Tingqi reviewed the report and questioned the three defendants and approved the detention until the 16th of this month for further questioning.

Impersonating Public Works Bureau Employee for Extortion

Gao Zhengqi and Wang Zhengnan Await Sentencing

Gao Zhengqi, a Jiangbei servant in the Public Works Bureau's Sanitation Department on Yulin Road, colluded with Luo Decai at a shed near Yanshan Road and Qiwu Street on the afternoon of the 5th of this month. He demanded two yuan in "dismantling fees" from Zhou Tongren, a pig farmer from Yancheng, and took a pig's head. The case was discovered, and he was arrested and sent to the First Special District Court for questioning and detention. Yesterday morning, Judge Zhao Linyu held a hearing for further questioning. The police lawyer Zhang Tianyin stated that the case was being rescheduled and that Gao Zhengqi had been found to have impersonated a Public Works Bureau employee on the 23rd of last month. He went to the Dai Tongxin noodle shop at 350 Yangshupu Road, claiming that there was an fee to obtain a license, of fifty yuan. As a result, his friend Wang Zhengnan mediated and paid ten yuan. However, Gao Zhengqi admitted to this money at the police station. Chu Kunfa, an inspector from the Sanitation Department, obtained eight yuan, and Chen Ronggao, a worker, obtained one yuan. He only got one yuan, but he had no right to investigate licenses in shops. Today, the Sanitation Department's foreigner and Chu and Chen had all come to court to testify. Dai Tongxin then testified that the defendant Gao Zhengqi came to extort money that day, taking ten yuan, etc. Chu Kunfa testified that he was an inspector in the Sanitation Department and had to be accompanied by a foreigner to investigate licenses in shops. The defendant's statement was completely false. Chen Ronggao also denied getting one yuan. When questioned, the two defendants were evasive. After reviewing the statements, Judge Zhao ordered them to be returned to custody and scheduled a sentencing date.

Wounded Soldier Dies of Illness in Shanghai

Lu Rongxiu, a soldier from the Third Company of the Second Supplementary Regiment of the 19th Route Army, from Guangdong Province, twenty-two years old, was wounded on the front lines during the anti-Japanese war in Shanghai. He was transferred to the Third Hospital in Changzhou for treatment. After recovering, he went to Nanjing to report to the 19th Route Army Headquarters' Beijing Office. On the 8th of this month, he received a certificate for wounded and sick officers and soldiers returning to their units (No. 616), a route schedule (from Nanjing to Shanghai to take a boat to Xiamen to return to his unit), and a certificate to exchange for a boat ticket. He took a train from Beijing to Shanghai. Unexpectedly, after arriving in Shanghai, he suddenly fell ill. He went to Renji Hospital for treatment, but unfortunately, his illness was too severe, and he died two days ago. Since there are no family members, the hospital notified Tongren Yiyuan Branch to prepare a coffin for burial and wait for family members to claim him.

World Bank to Move to New Building Tomorrow

The World Bank's new three-story building at 140 Fuzhou Road, Zhongshi, has now been completed and is scheduled to officially move in and open on the 14th of this month. It is reported that during the relocation anniversary period (from the 14th of this month to the 14th of December), the interest rate on lump-sum deposit savings and commercial time deposits, regardless of the term or amount, will be increased by one percent. For amounts of 300 yuan or more, in addition to the increased interest rate of one percent, a desk calendar with a stand for the next year or a copy of the "Encyclopedia" will be given as a gift. For all other types of deposits, regardless of whether they are new or old accounts, and regardless of the amount, a wall calendar will be given as a gift to commemorate the occasion.

Russian Beggar with a Mute Girl

Truly Incomprehensible

Yesterday afternoon, at approximately 1:00 PM, Police Officer Zhang Yinian of the 24th post of the First Section of the First District of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, found a Russian beggar named Fei Xilifu (transliteration) in Da Wang Miao Street in the South City, carrying a young girl of about ten years old. They were acting suspiciously. The police officer immediately brought the two of them to the station. During the preliminary hearing by the director of the station, because the two sides could not understand each other's language, the Russian beggar Fei Xilifu could not explain the origin of the girl. When the girl was asked, she was a mute, speaking incoherently and gesturing, which was incomprehensible. Because one was a foreigner and the other was a mute, the case could not be investigated. An official document was prepared and sent to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for investigation.

Jiang Jinshi Injured While Calling for Help from Robbers

At the home of Jiang Jinshi, wife of Jiang, at 869 Hongxing Lane, North Nicheng Bridge, at around 3:00 PM yesterday afternoon, six thugs wielding handguns arrived. They threatened and intimidated her, and then grabbed a gold bracelet and gold ring from her arm. Jiang, unwilling to accept this, shouted "robbers." Fearing the arrival of detectives, the robbers fired a single shot, injuring Jiang's head. Bleeding profusely, the robbers fled in a swarm. Afterwards, neighbors reported the incident to Street Constable 2516 of the Laozha Police Station, who arrived on the scene and transported her to Renji Hospital for treatment.

Why Die if You Can't Have Children?

Jin Zirui's Wife Commits Suicide

Yesterday at 3:10 PM, Police Officer Liu Junde of the Zhabei Tanziwan police station discovered that Jin Zirui's wife had committed suicide by hanging at number 29. He took Jin to the station, who claimed, "My wife has not been able to have children for more than ten years, and the two children we adopted have also died one after the other. So, in frustration, she committed suicide by hanging. There was no quarrel or beating." After reviewing the statement, the district chief asked him to provide a guarantor and await examination.

Warehouse Shortage Acknowledged

Bu Nei Men Company, which specializes in importing alkali, pigments, fertilizer powder, and other goods, had a large number of goods arriving. Moreover, the Zhaofeng Road warehouse was being renovated, so the alkali was stored in the various warehouses at the Blue Funnel Wharf. The number stored in Warehouse 7 was initially over 30,000 packages. In recent months, the goods have gradually been removed, and as the goods were coming close to completion, a careful inspection revealed a shortage of more than 480 packages. It is feared that the goods were wrongly delivered to customers on Saturday afternoons. However, the Blue Funnel Warehouse 7 is willing to take responsibility for the compensation. Bu Nei Men's new warehouse has now been completed and will no longer deposit arriving goods in other warehouses. It is reported that the wharf warehouse also lacked over 400 packages of foreign rice in 1927. This is the second time.

Zhu Zong's Young Daughter Found by Qingpu Police

Wang Xu, a widow from Pudong living in a pavilion at 7 Fangxie Road, Old West Gate, has a ten-year-old daughter, Wang Yaomei, who attends school at a primary school in Xiaoximen. Yan Maosheng, a fellow villager, often visited her. Because of the relationship with the village, the woman did not find anything to be amiss. Unexpectedly, Yan took advantage of an opportunity to abduct her daughter Yaomei under the pretext of seeking flower associations in the countryside. Then, he delivered the girl to the Xuyi Quan of Bai Mayi in Nanyao to sell to Qingpu. When it was discovered by the Nanyao police team of Qingpu County, Xu and Yan's actions were deceptive. They were immediately detained and escorted to the team headquarters by Team Leader Bian Jingcheng and Special Agent Shu Changsheng for interrogation in detail. Yan Maosheng frankly admitted that he had abducted her from Shanghai. Team Leader Bian Jingcheng prepared a letter to inform the mother to come to Qingpu to identify her daughter. Wang Xu, bereaved of her beloved daughter, the only daughter and the bone remains of her husband, was crying and wishing to die. Receiving this letter, she smiled through her tears and rushed to the Nanyao police team of Qingpu County. The mother and daughter were reunited. The police team leader, in light of Wang Xu's loneliness and poverty, did not allow the woman to spend a penny on all expenses. Therefore, the mother and daughter did not stop praising the benevolence of Team Leader Bian.

Inspection Report of the China Agricultural and Industrial Bank

The issuing treasury and the operating treasury of the China Agricultural and Industrial Bank have always been completely separated. According to the bank's articles of association, the cash reserve is more than 70% and the guarantee reserve is less than 30%. On the 12th of this month, after inspection by accountant Wang Zikang together with the supervisory board representatives Xu Jilu and Xu Busun, the results were as follows: The total amount of exchange coupons issued was 4,885,000 silver dollars. The total amount of exchange coupon reserve was 4,885,000 silver dollars, including 3,911,388 silver dollars in cash reserve and 973,612 silver dollars in guarantee reserve. The above two items show that the cash reserve accounts for more than 80% and the guarantee reserve accounts for less than 20%. This report is hereby made.

In addition, there were football, tennis, volleyball, and basketball matches in the gymnasium and the school's lawn. Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated: Shandong and the coastal areas here will have clear and cold weather with strong or very strong northerly to northeasterly winds. The East China Sea will have cloudy and rainy weather with strong northeasterly winds. Southern Taiwan and the Miyako Island area will have cyclone rain. The Yangtze River basin will have cloudy weather with fog in the morning and uncertain wind direction. The hurricane center was located within 60 miles of the intersection of 20 degrees north latitude and 122 degrees east longitude at around 2 PM, moving north with strong winds. Also, within the 24 hours before 3 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this port was 60.8 degrees, and the lowest was 45.1 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest temperature was 65.3 degrees, and the lowest was 58.3 degrees.

Special Article

Judge Fessenden's Report on the Shanghai International Settlement, Volume 4 (21)

(1) Amendment of the Land Regulations

26. If proceeding according to the suggestions already made to amend other aspects of the Land Regulations, it would be clearly appropriate to seize this opportunity to delete the appended conditions of Clause 24 of the Land Regulations, so that the Board of Directors would be free from restraint, and would not need to obtain the approval of the taxpayers' meeting regarding matters related to staff members, so that the policy contained in the existing pension plan could be carried out to its logical conclusion. In this way, the position of some staff members would be the same as that of civil servants. If this could be achieved, then a rule could be established to stipulate that only those within a certain grade, that is, those listed in the "permanent" staff roster, could be included. The main provisions that can be included in this rule are briefly described in an appendix to this report by me. (Note 9)

27. It may be noted that, although the proposed provisions are intended to limit the power of the Board of Directors to dismiss staff members before they are eligible to receive what is now called the "minimum pension," there are various reasons other than misconduct of staff members, that should allow the Bureau to continue to exercise this power, but a portion of the pension or other remuneration calculated in proportion to the years of service, must be given to the staff member. In this regard, the power of the Board of Directors to deliberate and handle the matter is indeed broad. Some people may think that the word "permanent" does not apply to services that must be controlled by such rules, but the principles included in this plan, if recognized, should obviously greatly improve the current status of the Bureau's staff members within the scope of the plan regarding tenure security.

The outstanding question regarding any such plan is how to establish a reasonable tenure security for the personnel employed, and how to protect the Board of Directors, so that it is not burdened by the incompetence or unsuitability of staff members in handling affairs. The so-called incompetent or unsuitable staff members are those who are generally incapable of handling affairs, or whose positions are not suitable for their abilities.

28. One of the main features of the above-proposed method is that a municipal service committee should be specially organized, one of its tasks is to investigate permanent staff members who are accused of misconduct. If the result of the investigation shows that the staff member is indeed guilty of misconduct, and should be dismissed, demoted, or have their salary reduced, the Board of Directors should follow suit. If a permanent staff member is to be dismissed by the Board of Directors for reasons other than misconduct, the staff member may request that the proposal be submitted to the committee for consideration, but the dismissed staff member, if still able to receive a portion of the pension or other remuneration calculated in proportion to the years of service, the Board of Directors is not bound by the committee's report, and may handle the report after considering it, in accordance with what it deems appropriate.

29. Staff members who are dismissed and have their pensions and retirement savings confiscated are recognized as clearly different from those who are dismissed without such confiscation. Although staff members have the same right to request the committee to intervene in events regarding the latter, as in the former, in events not involving the confiscation of rights, the Board of Directors is free to deliberate and handle the matter after considering the committee's report.

In addition, there are several other tasks that the committee may be asked to undertake, which will be described below.

(2) Resolution of the Taxpayers' Meeting

30. If the Land Regulations cannot be amended in the near future, the second way to solve this problem is for the taxpayers' meeting to pass a resolution at any time, so that the Board of Directors can obtain the recognition of the taxpayers in accordance with the provisions of Clause 20 of the Land Regulations, and apply special service conditions, such as those suggested under heading (1), to staff members whom the Bureau wishes to include in the permanent roster. In this way, the Bureau can have a standard to sign contracts with relevant staff members, without being restricted by the three-year term stipulated in the existing Land Regulations. (Note 10)

(3) Amendment of the Pension Regulations

31. The proposed third method is only to amend the pension regulations, so that staff members who are entitled to pension benefits, if they leave before reaching the age at which they can enjoy the minimum pension stipulated in the existing pension regulations, can receive a portion of the pension calculated in proportion to the years of service within certain restrictions. (To be continued)

Free Talk

Two or Three Words

Do Chrysanthemums Match Reclusive Hermits?

— Zhan Lu

Any literati can effortlessly recite Zhou Maoshu's saying: "Chrysanthemums are the recluses of flowers." Therefore, upon seeing chrysanthemums, literati automatically consider themselves to be facing a reclusive hermit, and all published works invariably regard chrysanthemums as hermits. Alas! Do chrysanthemums match reclusive hermits? I don't think so.

If chrysanthemums match reclusive hermits, then, in the past two months, one could meet hermits anywhere. Go to a teahouse for tea, and there are hermits; go to a restaurant for drinks, and there are hermits; go to a theater for a play, and there are hermits. These hermits are at everyone's beck and call, moving east when told to move east, and moving west when told to move west, solely because they have abandoned their homeland by the eastern fence and specialize in bustling places to provide flowery embellishments to life. If Zhou Maoshu were alive today, he would certainly not call them hermits among flowers, but rather call them politicians among flowers.

Sometimes, a grand chrysanthemum exhibition is held, with all sorts of labels inserted in the chrysanthemum pots; it is just like holding a grand meeting of politicians, with diverse political views, all wearing badges on their chests. Alas! Chrysanthemums, chrysanthemums, your political color is a bit too strong!

From chrysanthemums, I also thought of the willow catkins of spring; people call willow catkins frivolous, but they are not. Willow catkins are martyrs among flowers. Once the spring is gone, willow catkins flutter away from the trees, unafraid of being crushed to pieces, stained with mud, and entering the water, determined to share the same fate as the spring; this spirit of sacrifice is worthy of our respect.

Rather than appreciating the politician-like chrysanthemums, it is better to worship the martyr-like willow catkins.

Ailments of the Times

— Ke Ding

丨Manifestation and Relief after Circumcision丨

In your right hand, you hold a foreskin-like thing, stuffing it full of old newspapers, thinking you are hiding doctoral and master's diplomas from Tokyo, New York, London, Paris... advertising that you truly understand the languages of Japan, America, Britain, France... Thus, you spread it before your friends under your sway, how they foolishly listen and admire. As for you! How proud and self-satisfied you are!

Frogs frolic and sing on the lotus leaves in the lotus pond, how full of natural interest! At this time, a water buffalo comes along, it drinks water by the pond; somehow it aroused the frogs' interest in comparing bellies with the buffalo. Think, how much bloating ability does a frog's belly have, finally bloating the thin and tender belly to pieces. 丨Earning the ridicule and insults of its kind!

Do you want to be a frog? I think it is best not to reach the point of splitting your belly like a frog!

××××××

The pig locked in the fence, getting sustenance from its owner, is complacent and sleeps soundly. It often makes a few deep nasal sounds in a dazed state, never thinking about how far and deep its future is, or the gains and losses. Even during the day, it is generally asleep, unless it is time to eat.

The young masters who inherit their ancestors' estates also know that the pigs locked in the fence have the same symptoms, but they also have the same fate. Think, in this modern era where might prevails and justice is neglected, perhaps someone will come to take a share of your pie. If you resist, I am afraid you will taste the final 丨same fate as the pig丨

Do you want to be a fruitless pig? I think of course not, then please go at full speed on the "road of righteousness!"

Funny Talk about Minor Marriages

— Jin Butong

丨Deceiving and Being Deceived丨

Once, I had a classmate who wanted to find a spouse, not aiming too high, not settling too low, after five or six years, even matchmakers disappeared. He was worried about the three unfilial acts, the greatest of which is having no offspring, so he came up with the whimsical idea of ​​posting a marriage advertisement in the newspaper. After three days of advertising, he took a trip to the newspaper's mailbox and actually retrieved seven response letters. He was so happy that he couldn't close his mouth, thinking that among these seven letters, he could always find a wife who was eight-tenths to his liking. How could he know that it would almost take his breath away after reading them. One letter said, "If you want a wife, go to Qinglian Pavilion to find one." (Qinglian Pavilion is where the most low-class prostitutes in Shanghai are.) One said, "Wait until I marry and have children and then marry you." One said, "This is my small portrait, what do you think?" Enclosed in the letter was a calendar girl picture. One said, "My old nanny is not bad looking, 62 years old, willing to introduce her to you." The remaining three letters were similar, all trying to have fun, and for a time, it became a laughingstock among friends.

Later, his classmates, seeing him getting older day by day, advised him to compromise and get married. So, with the help of a friend, he married a lady. But he was still upset after the last incident, so he posted a female advertisement seeking a spouse for one day, and received a total of twenty-two letters. He cut them open one by one to read them. Each letter had a photo attached, some of which were artistic photos. There were seventeen wearing suits, four in casual clothes, and one in military uniform. The one in military uniform was a staff officer. In the twenty-two response letters, all uniformly reported their age, place of origin, education, and occupation. The least amount of family property was 10,000, and the least monthly income was 80. The words in the letter were more gentle than lambs. My friend laughed haha after reading each letter. In the end, he returned them one by one. He said to me, "This time, I took revenge." For a time, it became a laughingstock among friends again.

Slogans of Country Folks

— Rong Yu

丨Contradictions and Injustices of Urban Life丨

In the splendid city, the houses seen are tall and towering, with electric lights shining brightly; the streets walked are flat and wide, with bustling traffic; the people encountered are dressed in bright clothes, covered in perfumes, and everything else is aristocratic and modern, enough to make country folks dizzy. But there is also another side! Pigeon-cage-like rooms, where a family of all sizes lives, sleeping and eating there; even urination and defecation are done there. This also makes country folks strange, because the economy has reached this point, which cannot be found in the countryside. Even beggars who are so poor that they don't have "a tile to cover their heads" are more comfortable cooking casseroles in the temple of the earth. The living conditions of Shanghai people are truly unfair, the good ones are better than jade pavilions and jade buildings, the bitter ones are not even as good as pig pens.

Whether it's noon or night, no matter which road you walk on, your nose always smells a cooking fragrance, making your mouth water. Arousing the curiosity of country folks, he carefully investigated. Shanghai people's eating habits are indeed diverse and their taste is good. Speaking of foreign food, there are British, American, French, Italian, German, Japanese, and Russian styles. Speaking of Chinese food, there are Beijing style, Sichuan style, Fujian style, local style, and many other styles. If you stay in each restaurant and taste various flavors, I am afraid it will take a year to complete. Just as the country folks were admiring it, they suddenly saw a meal carrier passing by, and a few small rice-grabbing heroes jumped out of the alley to pour away the leftovers. The country folks then thought: those who eat, eat, those who are hungry, are hungry, one has so many styles and the other is suffering from hunger.

The clothes worn by those in suits, the country folks cannot name the fabric, but he knows very well that it comes from abroad, and an inch of the price is worth more than ten feet of old cloth in the countryside! Not to mention the clothes of modern girls, just take her feet to calculate, high-heeled leather shoes are imported goods, costing dozens of taels of silver; pure silk socks also cost a few taels of silver. The country folks thought: these coins in the countryside can build a thatched house, which can indeed accommodate several people, but now it is not enough to be trampled on by their feet for a month. The country folks couldn't help but secretly feel envious, but as he walked past a large wall, he saw a few brave heroes desperately tearing off the posters on the wall, preparing to use them as coats to resist the sharp northwest wind, and he secretly admired them again.

When country folks arrive in Shanghai, what he sees is contradiction and injustice. He is angry and hates it, so he also shouts slogans: the countryside is a fair, simple, and pure place. Come to the countryside!

Short Messages

The female poet Yu Xiuyun is the granddaughter of Mr. Yu Qiaqing, a well-known figure in Shanghai. Today (the 13th), she will hold a wedding ceremony with Mr. Chen Xianmo at the Datong Hotel. Yu and Chen played important roles in the play "The Merchant of Venice" two years ago. In the play, Chen proposed to Yu, and now it has become a reality, a truly good story. When Chen and Yu got engaged, the author of "Three Love Songs," Zeng Jinke, filled in the words to "Hao Shi Jin" to congratulate them, and now he has filled in the words to "He Xin Lang" to congratulate them. The words mention the two people's acting and marriage proposal in the play, and the words are fresh and lovely. The words say: "Like jade, a pair of shadows stand tall and upright in the pavilion, tying the knot of a hundred-year alliance. Thank Shakespeare for being so affectionate, secretly tying the red silk thread. This matchmaker is hard to find in the world. The osmanthus is fragrant and the weather is fine, don't waste the good time in vain. Ask Lang to tidy up the clouds." "Is the old story of the stage still remembered? Selling the coffin was a fluke! Predestined relationship can be proven. Today's marriage has become real, both are fortunate to have three lives. From now on, mandarin ducks will share the same fate. Ashamed to watch the auspicious ceremony on this auspicious day, there is nothing to hold as a gift: I will give a word as a gift." In addition, Gu Zhongyi, the translator of "The Merchant of Venice," also has a congratulatory poem saying

Free Talk Editorial Department

The Poor Taoist's Death (13)

— Fan Yanqiao

4. Inerasable Scars

In her solitary life, Aigu also thought about her late husband Liu Agen in Cuiwei Village. She also disliked his rough black skin, loose braids, loud voice, and clumsy hands and feet, and it was difficult to recognize him as a lifelong partner. So, find another way out. She is only nineteen years old this year, and her precious youth has not yet passed, how can she stay inactive for a long time. Move, how to move? Which way to move? All sorts of questions often surged in her mind. During the day, newly acquainted sisters came to chat, and at night, she felt an unusual loneliness, and everything in the past kept coming to her mind.

She, who had no experience as a housewife, and had no productive capacity, had spent more than 130 yuan in three months. She then knew that what Lawyer Xia had said to her, "The monthly interest is enough for food and clothing," was a lie, a piece of candy to deceive her into agreeing to a divorce. Now, the outer edge of this candy is gradually disappearing, and the core is bitter. But she had already drawn a "cross" on a piece of paper, and she also knew that this was an ironclad proof that could not be changed in any way. Since she could not develop from this, she had to open up sources of income in other areas, because 30 yuan a month was the minimum, and she could no longer cut costs.

From the mouths of her sisters, she learned about their ways of making money. Apart from those who had husbands and relied on their husbands for support, the perfume, silk stockings, snacks, and gambling capital for playing mahjong were all earned by their own instincts and means. Although she had no hesitation about her chastity, and wished she could bite off a piece of flesh from the ungrateful Han Muliang, how could she care about his face, especially since he had already issued a statement in the newspaper severing ties. However, she felt too much bitterness from mixing day and night in the false and tentative manipulations of getting acquainted with strangers and drifting from one relationship to another. Therefore, she still did not dare to step into the threshold of this den of depravity, hovering outside the den, but she was unwilling to give up easily.

This strange news has been published since August 11th. ○Cut down and staple into a book. ○Time to browse ○ has infinite interest

Gold Market Reaction

Price Drops by 6 Taels and 4 Mace

After several days of consecutive gains, the gold market suddenly weakened yesterday. The price retreated from the 750 tael level. Dealers were hesitant, with fluctuations limited to about one tael. The range from morning to noon was no more than 3 taels and 6 mace. Overall, this was a reaction to the consecutive days of gains, with a total drop of 6 taels and 4 mace. The initial drop was sharp, driven by a surge in British and American exchange rates, a slight decrease in large silver bar prices, and a near-term rise in American silver, further impacted by continued growth in American cotton. Later, the price seemed to recover by two or three taels, mainly due to foreign exchange trends, with British exchange rate firm and American exchange rate stable, causing slight changes. Gold prices fluctuated around 46 taels. Different parties showed varying buying and selling intentions, with a sudden surge to 47 or 48 taels at the end. The Central Bank purchased 105 gold bars on the spot market at a price of 52 taels, sold by Tai Kangrun. As the market will be closed on Saturday, and considering the chaotic market conditions this week, fluctuating between weakness and strength, the range was significant. The lowest price at the beginning of the week was 734 taels and some mace, while the highest price at the end of the week was 753 taels and 7 mace. After a subsequent decline, the total range for the week was 19 taels and 4 mace. Overall, this was still an increase of 1 tael and 8 mace compared to the previous Saturday. However, the volatility was unpredictable. Details of yesterday's morning market are recorded below:

▲ Initial Drop of 8 Taels and 4 Mace The December market opened with a drop of 8 taels and 4 mace, at 744 taels and 7 mace. (Before the market opened, the unofficial trading of goods saw fluctuations, initially at 46 or 47 taels, then 3 or 4 taels, and later around 6 taels.) Afterwards, Zhifeng, Yongyuan, and Chun, among others, sold, causing an immediate rise of over 2 taels. This was due to purchases by Yuanmao, Yongheng, and Xing. When the foreign exchange market opened, it was flat. Then, the Korean market bought US dollars for the current month at 93.75, wheat firms offered 8.75, and Citibank bought January at 1.25, resulting in a price of 46 taels and 6 mace. Dadecheng and Yuanchun, among others, sold at 9:15 for 5 taels and 3 mace. Subsequently, the British gold quote contracted by 0.25, and the US dollar remained unchanged, resulting in a price of 47 taels. After 9:30, Hengyu, Yuantai, Yuanmao, Yong, and others bought, pushing the price from 6 taels and 8 mace to 7 taels and 3 mace. The domestic US dollar market strengthened, with January dollars available for sale at 30 yuan. Before long, Yuanxing, Yongfutaiheng, and general speculators sold, causing a retreat to 6 taels. At 10:00, Yifeng, Yongfeng, Hengyu, Zhaofengchang, and others eagerly bought, especially as November US dollars were priced at only 75, and the spread for February was 0.0625. This pushed the price up by 1 tael and 6 or 7 mace, reaching 47 taels and 7 mace by 10:10. Afterwards, Hengxing, Fuyu, Xiexingyong, and others heavily sold, causing a sudden drop in the market, falling by 2 taels. However, from 10:15 to 11:00, there was a slight recovery of a few mace. (Qian Changxiang bought, as it was opening for the Central Bank's spot purchase of 105 bars.) Subsequently, it was only 5 taels and 5 mace. Soon after, Yuanmao, Yongqian, and Changxiang bought again, and HSBC's absorption of February US dollars at 1.25 immediately pulled the price up by 1 tael and 2 mace. Hengxing continued to sell, and at 11:15, it retreated slightly by 1 tael, settling at 5 taels and 7 mace. Dadecheng, Bingxing, Yifengyong, and others increased their bids, adding another tael. At 11:30, it reached 6 taels and 6 mace. In an instant, retail investors came to sell, and Hengxing limited its sales, resulting in a price of 5 taels and 6 mace at 11:45. Soon, wheat firms absorbed January at 30 yuan, and Zhifeng, Yonghengyu, and others competed to buy, pushing the price up by another tael. By the close at noon, it was 46 taels and 7 mace, a drop of 6 taels and 4 mace compared to the previous day. Unexpectedly, goods and other items were suddenly added, pulling the price up to 8 taels. The highest price for half a day was 7 taels and 7 mace, while the lowest was 4 taels and 1 mace, a difference of 3 taels and 6 mace. Pure silver bars still added 10 taels and 2 mace and 5 fen.

▲ Discounted Price Mostly at 6 Taels The announced price remained at 814 taels, a discount of 67 or 68 taels. Later, it was 66 taels, 68 taels at noon, and 66 or 67 taels at the end, a discount of 6 taels more than the previous day. Book price was 49 taels to 47 taels, with a make-up price of 47 taels.

▲ Trading Fairly Active Trading on the exchange was not light. According to statistics, Yuanmao, Fan Changxiang, Yongfeng, Zhifengyong, Bingxing, Hengchangyong, Yuantai, Hengyu, Zhengfengyong, and Dadecheng Yuan Kangxiang all bought, while Taichang, Xiexingyong, Yuanxingyong, Futaiheng, Richang, Yuanchun, and Fuyu all sold. The Guangdong gang was slightly different. (Hengxing) sold 600-700 bars and bought over 200 bars. (Yifeng) bought 200-300 bars. These are the sales details reported by other firms.

Yarn and Cotton

Yarn Market Affected by the Environment

丨Many Rumors ··· Extraordinary Tightening of Silver Market丨

The cotton yarn market started rising and then fell. In the morning, the rise in US cotton caused retailers to cover short positions, and the market trend became firm. However, some manufacturers took profits. It was reported that demand was sluggish. In the afternoon, rumors suddenly arose in the market, and the news about the situation was not good, causing a change in atmosphere. It was also said that a large number of Tianjin yarns were coming to Shanghai. The market suddenly trended downwards. In short, the environment was too bad, and the silver market was unusually tight. Therefore, although US cotton rose, people's hearts were still not enthusiastic.

▲ Renbiao Continues to Fall 7-8 Mace In the morning market, Renbiao opened, rising with foreign cotton, and then fell back in the second and third sessions, eventually falling by 1-2 mace. In the afternoon, people's hearts suddenly changed. Due to the unfavorable atmosphere, prices fell by 6-7-8 mace in various months. The total transaction volume for the day was 28,500 bales. It was found that Jifeng sold 650 bales, Zhenda 550 bales, Changyu 600 bales, and Tonghe 1,550 bales, while Mingde bought 1,000 bales, Shenji 1,000 bales, Changfeng 750 bales, and Yicheng 500 bales. Cotton Market Rose in the Morning and Fell in the Afternoon

The cotton market rose in the morning and fell in the afternoon, but the US cotton continued to rise, and the market was still good, so people's hearts were tight. Later, in the afternoon, there were many rumors in the market, and the yarn market fell sharply, causing the related cotton market to fall as well. However, the demand from factories in the market gradually showed development, and although the prices in various producing areas fell, some had more firm intentions. The rising power of US cotton could be stabilized, and the cotton market may not fall.

▲ Zheng Biao's Situation of Weak in the Near Term and Firm in the Distant Term Zheng Biao opened in the morning, tightened due to the rise in US cotton, and rose by 1.5-2.5 qian in each month. In the afternoon, it fell by 1.5 fen following the yarn market. The total transaction volume for the day was 91,300 dan. It was found that Taichang sold 5,600 dan, Sanling 900 dan, Xie 4,200 dan, Changji 3,200 dan, and Mingde 2,400 dan, while Changfeng bought 5,900 dan, Juji 2,700 dan, Dejiang 2,000 dan, Gengfeng 2,000 dan, and Yuanda 2,600 dan. The closing prices are as follows:

US Cotton Covers Shorts

Continues to Rise Over 20 Points

Yesterday, US cotton rose strongly due to short covering, strong support from Wall Street, and buying. Futures prices rose by 17-23 points, and spot prices rose by 25 points. British cotton futures rose by 18-19 points, and spot prices rose by 16 points. Egyptian cotton spot prices fell by 2 points. Indian cotton initially rose with US cotton, but later weakened due to profit-taking by longs. Pingguoer rose by 4.25 rupees, Aubmra rose by 3.75 rupees, and Bai Luoxi rose by 5.25 rupees. The Trend of US Cotton in the Past Week Has Gradually Increased

A telegram from New York on the 11th reports on the cotton market in the past week: The cotton market initially rose due to the start of cotton transactions, strong sales of spot cotton, and a stable actual position. Soon, it rebounded due to active short selling and a large increase in the government's estimated report on Wednesday. However, when near-month prices were below 6 points, demand was strong, and the market was too soft, so short selling in the South became sluggish and the supply in the mainland decreased. According to statistics for the past week, the amount of cotton listed in the week was less than the previous week. Therefore, some experts believe that the weakness of the market has passed, and the industry's needs have decreased when buying is active. According to another source, a large number of November shipments need to be covered. The weekend statistics are appended below (in thousands of bales):
