Grain Market: River Down Rice Market Deteriorating Daily

Yesterday, there were still many ships arriving in the south of Shanghai, about 60-70. Retail sales in urban and rural stores were affected by the financial cotton market. Traders were even more miserable, so the market has been easing for days and sales are still difficult. As a result, people's morale is flagging, and the price of thick grain has fallen by another 3 jiao. Although the opening and closing prices were called yuan, they were falling step by step. The Ke-type rice merchants were slightly active, and the situation was stable. About 2,500 shi of River Down rice were opened.

▲ Yesterday, there were more than 40 ships arriving at Xinzha. There were very few transactions on the street. Changshu, Xibei, and Jiangyin rice were each 2 jiao lower. There was no boom or bust in thin rice. The arrival and sales of Budu sharp were balanced. Around 2,500 stone of River Down were opened.

Ke Xian Price Falls, Sales Brisk

丨Minnan Merchants Have a Stronger Appetite··· North Ocean Merchants Are Also Asking丨

Yesterday, the foreign rice market completely stagnated. Ke Xian has not continued to arrive, but after the market price fell back, it has aroused the concern of Ke merchants. The appetite of Fuzhou merchants is stronger, and Tianjin merchants are also inquiring slightly. The market seems to be turning from weak to stable. A total of 100 bags of Jiangxi machine-milled late rice were sold at a price of 8 yuan 6 jiao. 109 bags of Hunan machine-milled yuan rice were sold at a price of 10 yuan. 436 bags of Hunan machine-milled oil rice were sold at a price of 8 yuan 8 jiao 5 fen to 8 yuan 8 jiao. 350 bags of machine-milled Jingjiang were sold at a price of 8 yuan 4 jiao to 8 yuan medium. Except for Xiang machine yuan, which was purchased by Tianjin merchants, all of them were purchased by Fuzhou merchants. The price continued to be 4-5 fen smaller than the previous day, 4-5 jiao smaller than the beginning of the month, and 7-8 jiao smaller than the highest market price. However, with the purchase of Min and Jin yesterday, the market situation may be stabilized.

Flour Futures Market Active, Market Stable

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, the prices of each month generally showed a flat and stable trend. Because there were no quotations for foreign wheat, the sentiments of both parties were calm. However, since the selling was not prosperous, the buying was still active, so although the initial opening was flat, it gradually became more profitable, and the prices of the recent months were slightly better. When the market opened in the afternoon, the major players' intentions were very firm. Because the prices in each period, near and distant, were clearly high and secretly active, they wanted to revive their morale. However, Nan Yang wheat has sold, and the number of lots issued by each dealer was about another 100,000 bags. However, people's hearts remained unmoved. Before the large buyers exhausted their resources, they would not let go. As a result, the price of this month rose by 7.5 li from the previous day, the price of December rose by 1.5 fen, the price of January rose by 2 fen, the price of February rose by 1.5 fen, the price of March rose by 1 fen 2 li, and the price of April rose by 1 fen.

Wheat Market Initially Stable, Then Steady

Yesterday, the wheat market opened in the morning and afternoon with prices for various months generally showing an initial stability followed by a steady trend. As there were no quotations for foreign wheat, market sentiment was lackluster. November and December remained unchanged, January and February did not open, March decreased slightly by three cents, and April decreased slightly by one cent. However, during the afternoon session, November to February did not open. March and April benefited from a good flour market, with rumors of a certain factory making large purchases, which improved market sentiment. Nevertheless, continued transactions in foreign wheat at favorable standards inevitably exerted downward pressure. Consequently, March decreased slightly by one cent, while April increased by one cent.

Sugar Market: Raw and White Sugar Prices Rise Slightly

丨Price Increase of 2.5 Cents丨

Yesterday, the sugar market saw a shift to better sentiment due to firm benchmark prices and a slight contraction in Dutch exchange rates. In addition, reports from Cuban telegrams indicated storm damage and potential losses in sugar production. As a result, the association's trading trends gradually tightened. No. 24 raw white sugar was priced at 14 taels and 8.5 cents, an increase of 2.5 cents from the previous day. Simultaneously, foreign firms also opened a batch of No. 24 raw white sugar spot goods following the trend. Huaxin sold 500 bags, and Changxing sold 1,700 bags, with prices matching the association's quotations. The quoted prices for No. 18 medium white sugar and Nos. 8, 9, and 10 Dutch red sugar remained unchanged. The market outlook has stabilized from weak due to an increase in incoming goods.

North-South Goods: Glutinous Rice Branch Land Prices Rise

丨Red Rice Sells Quickly Upon Arrival... Ordinary Goods Remain Popular丨

Glutinous rice branch: Recent arrivals of glutinous rice branches have been scarce, and the stock held by trading houses is also limited. As a result, the market outlook has entered a firm and stable position. According to letters from the production area, the procurement price has risen to 135 yuan, which translates to 85 or 86 taels in Shanghai, making it difficult to match offers. Therefore, there are few continued arrivals. Currently, high-grade glutinous rice branches in the market are selling for 80 taels, which is relatively cheap compared to other prices because these are goods that were acquired earlier with lower costs. Now that land prices have risen, the future market will inevitably follow higher.

▲Red Rice: Red rice was previously in short supply due to a milling shortage, and trading houses had long been out of stock. It is now known that various Chaozhou firms have recently received new shipments, which have been released in recent days. Top-grade "through-heart" red rice is priced at 29 taels, ke-grade red rice at 27 taels, and upper-middle grade at 23 or 24 taels. However, ordinary grades are selling better in the market because the northern river routes are about to freeze, leading to recent purchases. Prices have reached 18.5 taels, making them quite tight. Market stock is very scarce, and may need to be tightened further.

Silk and Tea: Customs Closure, Foreign Firms' Silk Market Inactive

Yesterday (the 12th) was the Premier's birthday, and the Jianghai Customs House was closed as usual. In addition, yesterday was the last day of the autumn races in the city and a Saturday. Most foreign firms were closed for the morning, and the foreign silk market was inactive.

Overseas Silk Market Summary

New York Italian Silk Imports Soar: The New York raw silk market has seen a surge in demand for high-quality Italian silk from silk mills due to the insufficient tensile strength of Japanese silk, which can easily break when used alone for silk weaving and must be mixed with raw silk from other countries. As a result, inventories are dwindling and imports are booming. The total quantity of Italian raw silk imported into New York last month (October) reached 2,851 bales, an increase of 1,931 bales compared to September.

▲US Raw Silk Sales Decline Last Month: The New York market was affected by the presidential election last month, and the silk market was sluggish, leading to a significant decrease in raw silk consumption. According to a telegram from the New York Silk Association yesterday, the total consumption of raw silk from China, Japan, Italy, France, and other countries in New York City last month (October) was 53,703 bales, a decrease of about 6,000 bales compared to September. Chinese silk and Italian silk each increased by 1,000 or 700-800 bales, while Japanese silk decreased by 7,797 bales.

▲Chinese Silk Prices Difficult to Rise in London: The London market has seen large shipments of Japanese silk products arriving, with exceptionally low selling prices, 50-60% cheaper than British factory products. This has resulted in a pile-up of goods in British silk mills and a significant decrease in raw silk consumption. Furthermore, the excessive dumping of cheap Japanese silk has made it difficult for Chinese silk prices to rise. The quoted price for top-grade white silk from factories is less than 600 taels per bale when converted to Chinese silver, and Tussah silk is only worth 550-560 taels.

Ping-Shui Tea Actively Sold in the United States

Yesterday, the foreign tea market in this city saw renewed activity in the sale of Huzhou Ping-Shui green tea to the United States. The Jardine Matheson and China Tea companies purchased a total of more than 2,500 boxes at a selling price of 44-45 taels, which was slightly firmer than before. The sales of Lu-grade green tea were also quite active. There were sporadic transactions in Wuyuan Tunxi Zhenmei tea. Needle and Xiu mei teas have seen some activity in the French market recently, with transactions also being conducted via telegram. However, the opening market prices still show a downward trend with no rise.

Hardware: Hardware Market Suddenly Sees a Rising Trend

Yesterday, the hardware market suddenly saw a rising trend. The reason is mostly due to the limited market supply and continuous customer sales. In addition, local factories in this street also need a lot of parts, and market conditions are exceptionally good. English steel plates, tinplate, new lead wire, small nails, ribbed steel, and new Yangguang goods have all increased in price, and sales are exceptionally brisk. It is reported that 6,000-7,000 dan were sold yesterday to customers from Tianjin, Yantai, Qingdao, and the Yangtze River area.

Pig Iron: Foreign Firms Already Active in Procurement

Foreign firms have recently started procuring Hunan pig iron, and the market is more active than before. Prices are rising due to the limited arrivals. The current market price is estimated at 255 taels per ton, an increase of 5 taels from before, and the market has exceptionally limited spot goods with very good market sentiment.

Tinplate: 5,000-6,000 Boxes Arrived Yesterday

There are widespread rumors in the tinplate market that there is a shortage of goods, causing general buyers to lament that there is nothing to buy. Yesterday, New Taikoo Wharf received a new shipment of 5,800 boxes, attracting a large number of buyers and resulting in many transactions. It is reported that Ba opened more than 1,000 boxes. With continuous arrivals in the future, there should be no shortage panic in the market. However, it is also reported that the current spot goods of the Boxer Indemnity Committee still have more than 20,000 boxes unsold, which is a hindrance to price increases. Serge Twill Sells Actively

Serge twill is a material specifically used for lining Western suits. Its sales are most brisk in the current cold weather. Domestic goods are also being produced, with a texture that is softer than imported goods and a silky, beautiful appearance because it is woven with rayon. Currently, a single-width bolt sells for 6.5 cents, and tailors who make Western suits are all buying it, which has greatly impacted imported goods. The selling price has fallen several times, and new orders from foreign firms have decreased sharply. Yesterday, the Serge twill market suddenly became very active, and the selling price rose again. The reason for the increase is the shortage of both arrivals and stock, with demand exceeding supply. Buyers are searching everywhere, causing the price to suddenly rise sharply. Wholesale discounts are 1 tael and 5 cents net per bolt, and retail is priced at 2.4-2.5 yuan per yard.

Riding Breeches Market Seen as Good

The market atmosphere at the recently organized woolen fabric trade association is quite good, and sales are very lively. The market for riding breeches is even better, with the public selling price continuing to rise. Kongsi, Luxun, and Hualun riding breeches are all selling for 6 taels and 1 cent, and sales are extremely brisk. Because market stock is dwindling, buyers are rushing to purchase. Lower-grade goods from the Hualun brand are selling for 5 taels, but most of them are only quoted and not actually available. Rongtai goods are selling for 5 taels and 7 cents, an increase of more than 1 cent from last week. The popularity of riding breeches and overcoats is at its peak in the last two years.

Coal: Boshan Coal Prices Unlikely to Improve

丨Shanxi Coal Water Transport Fee Increases by 8 Cents per Ton丨

Yesterday, 300 tons of Boshan coal were traded. The nominal market price appeared to increase by 2.5 cents, but in reality, due to excessive coal inventories and the very active Japanese coal market, the actual price remained at 9 taels and 7.5 cents. More than 100 tons of Yuesheng coal were traded yesterday, but the market price did not improve, with sales at 10 taels per ton.

▲Shanxi white coal prices have been gradually rising recently, and it is reported that a large batch of new goods, about 4,000 tons, will be shipped in the next two to three days. It is said that the overall price will need to rise further, with screened lump coal needing to be 16 taels at the customs clearance and run-of-mine coal needing to be 15 taels. The reason for the firm prices is that the water transport fee for this shipment has increased by 8 cents per ton.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Speech

Brand Awareness

— Buddha

|The Eighth of the Art of Living|

The ancients spoke of "choosing the capable and employing them," or "using talents appropriately," and so on. These sayings have now become a thing of the past and are no longer applicable. What is most applicable now is the phrase "brand awareness." The phrase "brand awareness" was probably invented in the lower classes of Shanghai, but it has become an abstract noun in all levels of society. It contains profound truths and can be applied everywhere, which is why it is so good.

Today I went to have a drink with some friends, but all the famous brands like "British Brand" and "Beijing Store" lamb cake and bean curd soup were associated with my friends. Yesterday I had a fight with Little Sanzi and suffered a great loss. Today I went to invite an old man, a "tycoon," to come out and show off a few connections to regain face. This is also a strong use of brand awareness. Therefore, the stronger the brand, the better, and the more, the better. With a brand, you don't have to worry about losing face.

This is the case in Shanghai society, and it is also the case in various associations. If you want to eat, you must first establish brand awareness. If you want to save face, you must also establish brand awareness. However, there are many levels of brand awareness. There is heavenly brand awareness, earthly brand awareness, human brand awareness, and personal brand awareness. In the past, the Ban family's "Table of People" was divided into nine ranks. Now, if we were to divide brand awareness into detail, there would be far more than nine ranks. Assuming that you are associated with heavenly brand awareness, you will naturally have inexhaustible wealth, foreign houses, and cars at your disposal. Even if you only have personal brand awareness, you won't have to worry about the seven necessities of life. Therefore, establishing brand awareness is of utmost importance.

Puyi established brand awareness with the Japanese and became the ruler of a puppet state. His brand can be said to be strong, but he did not gain any real power and was at the mercy of the Japanese. Although his brand was strong, it was useless and he was merely scolded as a "puppet," a "traitor," and a cold-blooded animal. Our country has established brand awareness with the League of Nations, hoping to ask them for help, but it turned out to be a paper tiger. Although the surface is strong, it is actually not. After establishing it, there is still no sound or smell. The brand still cannot be established. This shows that establishing brand awareness is not an easy task. First, you must have a brand to establish, and then you must establish it properly for the brand to be useful.

Small brands establish brand awareness with big brands, and big brands establish brand awareness with particularly old brands. This is the only genuine, strong brand that cannot be divided. Establishing brand awareness back and forth is quite a sight to see.

Science

Simple and Easy-to-Make Small Toys

— Ke Quan

Recently, I have been conducting experiments on the center of gravity and have successfully manufactured several physical instruments. These instruments are also children's toys. Usually, they are made of wax or wood. Schools buy these instruments for experiments, and each one costs more than one yuan. Children need to pay several jiao for small toys. However, most of these things still come from foreign countries. If we manufacture them ourselves, it will only cost two or three jiao. If we can utilize waste materials, we can even make them without spending a copper coin. Since this is the case, we should manufacture them ourselves. Why spend money to buy foreign goods? Therefore, I dare not keep my knowledge a secret and will now write down the simplest, easiest-to-make, and most easily successful methods below:

We only need to prepare an eggshell and a little soil to start making a roly-poly toy. When eating eggs, make a small hole in the small end and pour out the egg white and yolk. Then, take this unwanted eggshell, fill it with soil, and paste several layers of paper on top of the eggshell. Then, use a brush to draw eyes, ears, and whiskers on the tip. This will become a roly-poly toy.

This roly-poly toy can be made without spending any money. It can be used to study physics or as a children's toy. Put it on a table and it can rock and sway. This is the effect of the center of gravity because the upper part is light and the lower part is heavy.

To make a galloping horse, first use a wooden board that is about seven or eight inches long, four inches wide, and one inch thick. Draw a horse shape on it and use a narrow saw to cut it along the drawn lines. Then, drill a diagonal hole in the abdomen and install a thick iron wire in the hole. Tie a heavy object (such as a small brick or stone) to the lower end of the iron wire to make the horse's hind feet rest on a horizontal rod. If it is balanced, make a clay ball based on the weight of the heavy object and attach it to the iron wire. After this is done, make another wooden frame to support the horse's hind feet, and it will become a galloping horse.

When you press this galloping horse with your hand, it will move up and down and will not fall down. It is indeed a very interesting toy. The physics behind this is that the horse's hind feet are the fulcrum on the wooden frame, but its center of gravity is below the fulcrum, not on the iron wire, but in the air below the fulcrum, which is on the vertical line of the fulcrum. This proves that if the center of gravity of an object is below the fulcrum, it will not fall even if the center of gravity is small.

To make a one-legged man toy, the method is even easier than making a galloping horse. Use a wooden board that is about seven or eight inches long, three or four inches wide, and one inch thick. Draw a human shape on it and use a narrow saw to cut it out. Then, drill diagonal holes on the left and right sides of the waist and install iron wires in the holes. The iron wires should be about two inches longer than the feet. Attach clay ball weights to the ends of the iron wires. Each of the two clay balls should weigh about three or four liang. Then, use another iron wire to pass through the shin, allowing it to be supported by both hands. Tie some broken grass and other things to both ends of the iron wire to resemble a person carrying a load. Then, nail a small nail under its upright foot. Use another piece of wood, round or square, and drill a hole in the middle of the wood. Install a wooden pillar in the hole and place its upright foot on the wooden pillar. It will be able to stand up. This is a one-legged man.

When you put this one-legged man on the wooden pillar and push the upper part of its body, it will sway left and right but will not fall down. It is even more fun for children to play with. The physics behind this is that its center of gravity is below its feet, so it will not fall even if the fulcrum is small.

University Hall! Such a Purpose! Sui Wan

School Photos

Chinese Language Teacher

— Xu Yu

While the students were sitting in the classroom, chatting and laughing merrily, Mr. Li, the impractical Chinese language teacher, walked in, carrying his lecture notes and striding with his splayed gait, causing everyone to feel disappointed.

Page 20

Several young men in Western suits and fashionable young ladies all expressed their contempt and disgust on their faces. In particular, Miss Huang even pretended to be disgusted and nauseous, spitting on the ground and taking out her fragrant handkerchief to cover her nose and look away, as if she was afraid that Mr. Li's shabby air would contaminate her.

But Mr. Li was always "tireless in teaching." He lectured in great detail and with great enthusiasm, and shouted loudly, "Chinese language is the language of the national essence. Its culture is so long and ancient that it cannot be compared to any other country in the world. Yet you, the younger generation, now disregard Chinese studies and are absorbed in the crab-like Western language. You speak Western languages and write Western languages. Is this not abandoning yourselves and following others? How can this culture not be swept away...?"

Mr. Li lectured endlessly, with saliva flying everywhere, but "the speaker was earnest, the listeners were indifferent." It seemed as if they were completely unrelated. Some students only cared about looking down at "The Fate of Tears and Laughter" and other novels with great interest, while others were concentrating on writing love letters. What was especially funny was that some were lying on their desks, snoring loudly, as if they were playing rhythmic music, harmonizing with the teacher's lecture.

And Ms. Wu, who was well-versed in Li Hanhui's novels, drew a portrait of the teacher with the title "Mr. ×××'s Precious Photo" and passed it around for everyone to see, causing a burst of laughter.

Although Mr. Li glared at the students, he finally "dared to be angry but dared not speak out." When the bell for the end of class rang, he hurried out of the classroom.

As a result, the silent and dreary classroom suddenly became lively again. Talking and laughing were heard everywhere. Miss Wang, who was dressed in Western clothes and exuded a Western air, was the first to refute the uselessness of Chinese studies, saying, "What is called 'national essence'? This is simply an outdated piece of junk. Otherwise, how could our Mr. Li, who is well-versed in the national essence and speaks nothing but 'zhi hu zhe ye,' be impoverished and sitting on the sidelines for the rest of his life? Sadly, his material reward is not even as good as that of an illiterate foreman."

Old Xu echoed, "That's right. It's the English language that has some prospects. Isn't our English teacher Mr. Liang's salary higher than Mr. Li's? Moreover, he also has a side job as a translator in a foreign company, earning several hundred yuan a month. This is so enviable..."

Just as he was speaking, Mr. Liang, the English teacher who aroused the envy of the students, arrived. He was wearing a very beautiful Western suit and carrying many gold-lettered Western books. He strode confidently to the podium. The students were all conquered by his extravagant Western air, and they all held their breath and listened attentively.

A Corner of Society

A Proud Man in Embarrassment

— Yong Jiong

The Value of a Match

I happened to meet Mr. Xu, whom I had not seen for many years, on ×× Road yesterday.

"Mr. Xu, long time no see, how are you?" I asked with a smile.

"Thank you, thank you," he replied with a nod and a smile.

After exchanging greetings, we stood and talked about our situations since our last meeting. According to him, he had just come from Nanjing. He told me a very interesting story, which I am now recording for the readers to read:

Today: I (Mr. Xu referring to himself) came on the early train, sitting in the first-class carriage. There were only me and a young man in a Western suit in the carriage. I felt very lonely and smoked a cigarette for entertainment, so I also put a box of matches on the table in front of me.

He looked alive, did not even say hello, reached out and took my matchbox, struck a match to light his cigarette, and then unceremoniously threw it back in front of me. At that time, I wanted to scold him, but after thinking carefully, I thought it would be better to pretend not to understand and use a trick to punish him.

When the train passed the ×× station, the train inspector had to check the tickets of the passengers to prevent any omissions. Just when they were checking my ticket, I pretended to be very calm and slowly opened the matchbox. "Huh! That's strange! My ticket was clearly hidden in this box, how could it be gone in an instant," I said, pretending to be very flustered.

He seemed to be taken aback, staring at me blankly without saying a word.

"There are only you and me in this carriage, no one else has come in. I seem to remember that you took my matchbox?" I asked, deliberately staring at him.

"I...I...I took it, but I didn't see the ticket," he replied, his face turning red instantly, stammering.

"The ticket was definitely hidden in this box, haha...joke...if no one took it, how could it be gone?" I pressed him further.

"Hurry, hurry, we have to go check elsewhere," the inspector urged impatiently.

"Okay...okay...I'll pay, I'll pay," he looked uneasy. He said to the inspector, "How much does it cost to replace a ticket?"

"In principle, a first-class ticket costs eleven yuan and one jiao. Now, if you want to replace the ticket, you will be fined double according to the regulations, for a total of twenty-two yuan and two jiao," the inspector replied pretentiously.

He gave the inspector the exact amount, replaced a ticket, and handed it to me. He looked very frustrated and stared out the window in a daze.

Short Story

The Patriotic Thief

— Rui Yucheng

The darkness had swallowed the earth; everything was clothed in mysterious black, and clear outlines were indistinguishable; only the flickering streetlights opened their sleepy eyes, trembling in the permeating night.

It was already close to midnight, and a barking sound came from the alley; it turned out that a blurred figure was swaying at the foot of the wall. The dogs seemed to have a snobbish mentality, and barked more and more vigorously at the poorly dressed figure, until he tiptoed into the gate of a house.

The house was actually not a residence, but an office; several writing desks were placed haphazardly in the hall, with fruit peels and chestnut shells scattered on the surface. Books, newspapers, stationery, and other items were covered with thick dust, lying on the desk, sick. The portrait of the Premier hung on the wall facing the entrance, and the national flag and party emblem hung diagonally on both sides. Half of the will had been torn off, and its full text could not be seen.

The figure entering the gate was undoubtedly a thief. He took out a flashlight and turned it on for a moment, saw the Premier's portrait, and bowed respectfully three times. Then he listened carefully, and a snoring sound leaked out from the room on the west side. He first looked around the hall, but could not find any valuables, so he quietly slipped into the room.

Occasionally, the person who had fallen asleep made a mumbling sound, and the thief then imitated a few cat meows. After about a quarter of an hour, he came out with a large number of clothes, looking anxious. He placed the clothes on the table, took a breath, and then turned on the flashlight to inspect them; he saw that there was a national flag and a party emblem in the clothes, and he hesitated; finally, he seemed to resolutely decide to send the national flag and party emblem back into the room.

With a loud crash, something fell and awakened the sleeping owner, who shouted, "Someone! Thief!" Then there was the sound of striking a match and the sound of someone getting up, and finally the sound of the thief begging for mercy was heard.

"Ah, spare me! If I didn't respect the national flag and party emblem and send them back to you, I would have escaped long ago! Everything is outside, nothing is missing; the original items are returned, so please forgive me!" His voice was very straightforward, and it was determined that he was definitely not an ordinary thief.

"Nonsense! Lies! Do you even know how to love your country? Do you even know how to respect the national flag and party emblem? Let me tell you honestly, many of the gentlemen working here are serving the party and the country. Can you, a thief, really love your country...?" After a burst of words, there was the sound of hands and slaps coming into contact.

"Ouch, don't hit me, I am indeed telling the truth! I am not willing to be a thief, wasn't I a graduate of a senior high school? I only blame the fact that there is no place to eat in society, and I don't have any older sisters or younger sisters to marry rich people; seeing that I was about to starve to death, I fell to this point! In fact, what about the 'revolutionary doctrine' and 'knowledge of party principles'? What don't I know...?"

"I don't believe your lies either. Because you didn't steal anything, I'll spare you this time; if I catch you in my hands next time, you won't have a good life! Get out!"

He walked out the door in a melancholy manner, and two lines of hot tears were visible on his cheeks under the moonlight. The dogs' barking sent him out of the alley, and it is unknown where he went to seek his livelihood.

Movie Special

Sunday, November 13th, Republic of China Year 21

Reader's Opinions

An Appeal for Children

— Zhang Yifei

In Shanghai, our children are so pitiful. There isn't a single cinema established for children, nor a single film screened for them.

Movies were originally a powerful tool for education. We should fully utilize them to develop their educational function, complementing and enhancing school education. However, while the theory is such, the reality is clearly before our eyes. Although Shanghai has many towering cinemas, if we examine them carefully, we can say that not a single one has educational goals.

The films they show are either "sensual" or "supernatural," with the former being more prevalent. They merely serve as entertainment for adults of the "leisure class," neglecting both the performance of cinematic art and forgetting the educational function of movies. It is almost a miracle to make a film solely for education and for children. Therefore, in Shanghai, it's nearly impossible to find films worth watching for children. Children are either rejected at the door or suffer adverse effects after watching them.

Because of their love for their children, general parents often take their children with them to the cinema when they go, to watch films that are really not suitable for them. As a result, the parents increase their own guilt, staining the pure and flawless minds of their children. That is to say, children receive bad education from bad or unsuitable movies, which may affect them for life.

Now, progressive countries in the world, such as England, America, Japan, and the Soviet Union, pay great attention to the educational function of movies, so the establishment of children's cinemas and the screening of movies for children are very common. Should our China lag behind other countries in this regard?

A few days ago, I saw in the newspaper that a children's cinema would be established in Shanghai. This may be true, or it may not become a reality. We can only wait for the future to confirm the truth of this news.

In short, in such a vast Shanghai society, there is a great need for movies for children.

Film Review

Talking about "Born to Love"

— Yan Nan

"Born to Love" is such a famous film, but after watching it, you might say, "It doesn't live up to its reputation." In reality, it is still a good film, but if our expectations for it are too high, we will find it bland.

The plot uses the European War as its background, following the same path as the silent "The Battlefield Flower" and the sound film "The Eagle Squadron." We have seen too many of these films, so we can't be too excited, which is also one reason why we find it bland. It tells the story of a woman whose lover goes to the battlefield, and the news of peace reaches London, but the news of her lover's death also reaches the woman's ears. She has no choice but to marry. Later, she has a child and learns that her lover is not dead, but has returned to England. Because of her husband's suspicion, she divorces, but her only beloved son is taken away by her husband, and her lover has already returned home. Soon, her lover returns a second time, but unfortunately, at the moment of their reunion, she gets her lover back, but her long-separated beloved son dies.

The story is like this. The first half is very loose, but the exciting part is entirely in the second half.

Constance Bennett is very good, for example, the scene of the divorce and the return of her lover both have very moving performances. Joel McCrea is also a good counterpart, but he has too few opportunities to perform. Paul Cavanagh plays a purely aristocratic Englishman and is very competent. The others have very few performances.

In many places, side writing and dark writing prove the director's skill and ability, which increases the power of the film. The photography and lighting are not bad, and there are several wonderful shots.

Constance's discovery of her son's death and the repeated pointing to the golden cross (a keepsake of their love) are both very noteworthy. The last few scenes are full of sorrow and gloomy fog, which further stimulates the music and gives the audience a deep stimulation when they leave.

This film seems too long, about more than 10,000 feet. There are many parts that can be cut, such as the description of the military hospital and the celebration of the peace memorial, which are extended to more than 300 feet, which is really too wasteful, while the European War Air Force is not filmed enough. The conclusion is that it is a very good film, but don't have high expectations before watching it.

International News

Preview of the Number of Films Produced by Countries Around the World in 1933

— A Friend

The United States Still Leads

Italy Ranks Last

Russia Has Silent Films

Our Country Has No Preview

The preview of new films from various countries from 1932 to 1933, the total number of films that have been decided to be produced is more than 1,500, which is another new record.

(First) The United States is still the world's hegemon in terms of the number of films produced. The films that have been announced to be produced, including various independent film companies, are almost 700, and 550 have been confirmed.

(Second) It is said that Soviet Russia will produce 440 films. Only 100 of them are sound films, and the remaining 340 are silent films with dubbing. The reason why Soviet Russia still pays attention to the production of silent films is to sell them internationally.

(Third) Germany is the third, with 150 films budgeted, preparing to be produced next year.

(Fourth) The United Kingdom closely follows Germany, preparing to produce 140 films.

(Fifth) The French photography studio also plans to produce about 90 films.

(Sixth) Wealthy countries have also announced that they will produce 20 films.

In summary, there are a total of 1,540 films. Apart from the 340 silent films in Soviet Russia, the remaining 1,200 are ordinary feature films in one language. Other short films and all productions that have not been formally announced are not included. When it comes to our country, there is no such systematic budget at all. Perhaps it is "unnecessary to do this"! Therefore, it is of course impossible to know how many Chinese films there will be in the 22nd year of the Republic of China!

Film Monographs

Smart People Who Are High-Eyed and Low-Handed

— Chen Dabei

The American "screen idol" Valentino once said, "Every one of the stars on the screen today is a young man and woman who used to work hard." Friends! Don't be misled by those unachievable words, thinking that stars are made by a licentious and romantic life. You need to know that hoping to become a star without working hard is a lucky thing in the pioneering era. If you want to show your skills in the future photography studio, you must train yourself hard!

Some people laugh at you, ridicule you, saying that your practice is in vain. Don't be afraid of him. I tell you that this society is intolerant! This society is full of a group of smart people who only criticize others and never do anything themselves. These smart people know that they suffer from a common problem, which is "high-eyed and low-handed." Only by criticizing others can they show their "high eyes." Only by not doing it themselves can they cover up their "low hands." These smart people are jealous of people who are progressing! They will not sympathize with those who work hard! The reason why all our Chinese careers are not as good as those in the East and West is because there are too many smart people like this.

Comrades who love art! Let me tell you honestly! It was him who crucified Jesus! It was him who wanted to murder Columbus on the Atlantic Ocean! It was him who did not allow Newton to prove that the earth is round! It was also him who shouted to overthrow Watt, who used steam to drive the machine! He is jealous of people's success! He likes people to fail! This society is full of such devils!

Silver Screen Star Dust

— He

These days, the air in Hollywood is filled with a thicker "romance," although many couples in the film industry have broken up in divorce court.

The latest and most talked-about information is about Estelle Taylor and Lyle Talbot. Lyle Talbot is a very handsome new movie star. We can see the pair of them everywhere now, but they both deny having any plans to marry.

Since Sean Harlow married Paul Bern, Joan Marsh is now the most sought-after and beautiful new star in Hollywood. She is currently in love with Bick Powell, who is the most moving singer in Blessed Event (a new Warner film, probably not yet screened in Shanghai).

Charlie Chaplin is currently immersed in a new love life. His object is the seductive Paulette Goddard. Do we want to see her? She will soon meet us in the new film "The Kid from Spain."

Tala Birell's recent fame is no less than that of Prince Ferdinand Lichtensteiu. Since the romantic history of Constance Bennett, Gloria Swanson, and Polax Negri was discovered, nothing has attracted more attention than her sacred love affair.

The sudden disappearance of Johnny Weissmuller and Luo Po Fan'er's love affair is just like their love, which broke out suddenly. Luo Po Fan'er vowed that she only favored one man, a prominent government official of a famous company, but the name has not been confirmed!

In the process of this pair of couples changing their love, people in Hollywood are stretching their necks, waiting for a season full of wedding events. At the same time, those stars who only want to be brides and not bridesmaids are hoping to get the first chair in preparing for many big weddings.

A Glimpse of the Racecourse Ballroom

— Mai

The other day, Xuan Jinglin, Li Minghui, and Xu Lai, three modern women, danced wildly in a ballroom by the racecourse. This night was a special banquet hosted by Miss Zhang, a Shanghai socialite, inviting them to dance. At the same time, Mr. Yan Gongshang, a senior executive of the Star Film Company, was also present, dancing madly with the dancers. Although he is over half a century old, his enthusiasm for dancing surpasses that of young people. His long beard flutters, and his long gown sways as he steps to the beat at will. Xuan Jinglin saw him and called him "Godfather," and danced past him with others.

Overseas Oddities

Movie Star Milk Bath

— Jieke

In the past, there was a baseless rumor in Shanghai that a concubine of our country's famous diplomat loved to take milk baths. It is said that milk baths have the effect of making the skin fair and the muscles plump. This rumor has never been verified. Now, movie stars in Hollywood are actually taking milk baths. We will soon be able to see it on the screen.

The scene of using movie stars to take baths to seduce the audience on the film was invented by the great director Cecil B. DeMille. For several years, he has made full use of this bath scene. Other directors have followed suit, adding a lot of color to the film. Recently, he even had the movie stars take milk baths, creating a new record in film history.

In DeMille's new film "The Sign of the Cross," there is a very large black marble Roman-style bath, filled with pure white milk. The movie star Claudette Colbert plays the licentious Roman Empress Poppaea, bathing in it. During the production, she floated in the milk bath naked for eight hours, creating the longest record for a bath scene in a film studio. However, it only lasts for a moment when it is shown on the screen.

When directing this bath scene, DeMille tried other white liquids, but they were not as good as milk in photography. Powder was probably harmful to Claudette's skin, so it was not used either. Later, 1,000 gallons of milk were poured into the huge Roman bath.

It is said that DeMille researched that Poppaea used donkey milk to bathe, so for the sake of authenticity, he also wanted to use donkey milk, but the audience could not tell the difference between donkey milk and milk, so he was a little careless.

Claudette is the first movie star to take a milk bath. She said that the women of ancient Rome were right, and milk baths do have a beautifying effect. After bathing in milk, she felt that her skin was soft and moisturized. Milk baths are too wasteful, she wants to use milk to wash her face and arms in the future.
